Yangzhou Land Tax Uprising

County Government Releases Arrested Villagers

Clearance Work Temporarily Suspended

(Zhenjiang) In the wake of the Yangzhou land tax clearance uprising, after repeated misunderstandings between the military police and the villagers, resulting in a bloody tragedy, the County Magistrate of Yangzhou agreed to the villagers' demands. On the morning of the 24th, 250 arrested men and women were released after signing guarantees. Another 19 people with more serious connections were detained for further handling. In compliance with the provincial order, he instructed his subordinates to temporarily suspend the clearance work. By noon, the villagers in the city and countryside had dispersed somewhat, and water and land transportation between the city and countryside and between Zhenjiang and Yangzhou had been fully restored. Of the seven bodies killed, two have not yet been claimed. Among the ten injured, one surnamed Zhu died on the 24th. The injured are seeking compensation from the government, which Chairman Wang of the Chamber of Commerce is trying to resolve. There are still some minor disturbances in the countryside. Village Chief Xiao Guangchao and his brother were beaten, and the houses of Chen Yuansong and Zhu Bing were destroyed because they did not participate in the petition. The county government is hiring workers to repair the damaged property, and the entire government staff is working through the night to sort out the damaged documents and deeds. The post-incident measures have been telegraphed to the province for instructions. (24th Dispatch)

Xu Tingyao's Division Builds Motor Road (Nanjing) After defeating the remnant bandits in western Anhui, Xu Tingyao's Fourth Division, in order to plan for local rehabilitation, in addition to disaster relief and tax and rent reductions, recently built a new motor road from Changtang to the Hekouji area to connect with the motor road between Huoqiu and Yejiaji, totaling over a thousand li. Supreme Court Intensifies Work

(Nanjing) The Supreme Court is hearing final appeals in civil and criminal cases. The files are complex, and the hearings take time. Previously, the judges of the court could only conclude a maximum of 12 to 13 cases per month. Recently, after President Ju's reorganization, the judges have been concluding more than 20 cases per month for several months, setting the highest record for the court's speedy case resolution. The work efficiency of the transcription section of the court's secretariat is also astonishing. In September, a total of 24 employees, excluding absences due to leave and illness totaling 28.5 days, transcribed 1,591,429 characters for the entire month, an increase of 450,000 characters compared to the previous month. (24th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Ministry of Foreign Affairs Selects Special Envoy to Siam (Nanjing) The issue of a treaty between China and Siam has been under negotiation between the two sides for ten years. After several twists and turns, no agreement has been reached. Recently, China promulgated regulations regarding the import of foreign goods and intends to send a special envoy to Siam to handle commercial affairs between the two countries. Jiang Zuobin, the minister to Japan, conducted negotiations with the Siamese minister to Japan. Later, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent Xie Xiang, the consul in Penang, to be responsible for handling matters in Siam. The matter proceeded very smoothly, and the Siamese government fully agreed to the establishment of commercial representatives. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs is currently selecting personnel to go. It is reported that the second step will be to negotiate and conclude a commercial treaty between the two countries, which will still be the responsibility of the Chinese and Siamese ministers to Japan. (24th Dispatch)

Foreign News

On the Far Eastern Question 4

Soviet Union Employs Clever Diplomatic Tactics

Leveraging the US-Japan Confrontational Situation for Bargaining Power

While Vigorously Bolstering the Chinese Communist Party's Strength

Although Temporary Harmony May Prevail, a Russo-Japanese War Ultimately Seems Inevitable

Tokyo dispatch from the National News Agency, 23rd: Observers here believe that Soviet Russia's Far Eastern policy is becoming increasingly clear, containing the following points: (1) Moscow will strive to dispel Japan's suspicions of Russia while simultaneously inciting Japan to suspect other countries, especially the United States. As evidenced by the recent article by Mr. Ledeck, chief editor of Izvestia, forcefully stating that if a dispute occurs between the US and Japan, Soviet Russia will remain completely neutral. TASS subsequently transmitted this article to Japan for widespread publicity, as proof of their intention. (2) While inciting Japanese militarists and the people to suspect the United States, Soviet Russia also continues to vigorously assist the Chinese Communist Party, hoping that the CCP will gain power in China and cooperate with Russia in the future. (3) Continuing to promote anti-Japanese sentiment in the United States to create conflict between Japan and the US, reaping the benefits of the conflict. (4) At this time, on one hand, indicating to the United States that if the United States still does not recognize Soviet Russia, Russia will be forced to cooperate, at least secretly, with Japan. On the other hand, indicating to Japan that if Tokyo does not respect Soviet Russia's interests and rights in Northern Manchuria and the ownership of the Chinese Eastern Railway, Soviet Russia will be forced to support the US's plan to not recognize territorial gains by force, including the non-recognition of "Manchukuo." Its skillful use of the US-Japan confrontational situation as a bargaining chip is a top-tier diplomatic strategy in the world and is likely to achieve great success. Regarding the situation last winter when the Japanese army advanced towards Northern Manchuria, Soviet Russia immediately amassed 300,000 troops near the Manchurian border. Diplomatic figures here uniformly stated that the Russian government's military action was purely for self-preservation, deeply fearing that an unexpected situation would lead to the Japanese army invading Soviet territory. Now, this fear has temporarily disappeared, so the Russian army has also withdrawn a portion of its forces. However, the troop deployment in areas bordering Manchuria has significantly increased compared to before. It is expected that it will continue to maintain sufficient strength to prevent adventurous militarists in the Japanese army from harboring desires for Russian territory. Furthermore, since the Northeast Incident occurred last year, half of Soviet Russia's diplomatic success has been due to the efforts of Ambassador to Japan, Troyanovsky. Mr. Troyanovsky, disregarding diplomatic conventions, often directly visited Army Minister Araki to inquire about everything and exchange opinions. He apparently convinced the Japanese General Staff that Soviet Russia would not interfere with Japan's plans in Manchuria, thus gradually easing the tense situation between Japan and Russia that was on the verge of erupting. Although the background of Soviet Russia's Far Eastern policy is its industrial plan, those Japanese who are familiar with international affairs all believe that once Soviet Russia completes its industrial plan and feels its strength can compete with the Japanese army, it will greatly change its attitude. A certain Japanese diplomat once said that both Japan and Russia desire to dominate Asia, which is an unavoidable reality in the future. The nature of the two governments makes it impossible for them to establish a long-lasting friendship. Sooner or later, one of the two countries will have to take second place, and this matter can only be resolved by force.

Japan Considers a Non-Aggression Pact with Russia

Proponents and Opponents Clash

The Emperor Listens to Hirota's Account of the Soviet Situation

Tokyo dispatch from the China United News Agency, 24th: The Japanese Foreign Ministry's policy towards Russia remains in turmoil, with proponents and opponents clashing. Regarding a Russo-Japanese non-aggression pact, arguments for and against continue to stand in opposition. Those who support a non-aggression treaty argue: (1) Those who oppose signing a non-aggression treaty have two errors: Firstly, they fail to distinguish clearly between international relations and domestic conditions; secondly, they view the Comintern's communist propaganda as the actions of the Soviet Russian government, thus generating unexpected terror. (2) Russo-Japanese relations are currently friendly, so a non-aggression treaty is unnecessary. However, to enhance Russo-Japanese friendship, what harm is there in signing one since Russia is willing to do so? Many countries in Europe have signed non-aggression treaties. (3) We cannot abandon Russo-Japanese friendship simply because Russia and Japan have different systems of government. (4) It is true that Russia's Five-Year Plan emphasizes military industry. However, Russia's military preparations are not necessarily solely aimed at Japan. Looking at the relations between European countries and Russia makes this clear. (5) Comintern's communist propaganda did not begin today. We cannot oppose a non-aggression treaty because of communist propaganda. Although Japan has tried its best to suppress it, the activities of the Communist Party remain fierce. Originally, communist propaganda is a domestic political issue, and preventing communism requires implementing good governance and remedying the shortcomings of domestic political and economic structures. Attempting to stop it with an international treaty demonstrates insufficient understanding. (6) A Russo-Japanese-"Manchukuo" alliance is acceptable if it proceeds based on the above reasons. Using our country's strength to prevent external forces is what constitutes vital diplomacy. Japan does not need to be overly afraid of Soviet Russia. If Russia has military preparations, then we will respond with full military preparedness, without overreacting. Those who oppose signing a non-aggression treaty argue: (1) Neither Russia nor Japan intends to invade the other's territory, so why sign a non-aggression treaty? Russia's deep desire for this treaty may be because Russia harbors intentions of invading Japan. (2) The Kellogg-Briand Pact already exists, so why draw a snake and add feet? (3) The Russian and Japanese systems of government are fundamentally incompatible. (4) There is a fear that the non-aggression treaty will cause the public's thinking on national defense to slacken and neglect military preparations. (5) Russia's Five-Year Plan primarily focuses on military industry and sees Japan as an enemy, and we fear falling into its trap. (6) Russia does not respect trust and continues to promote communism in Japan. We fear that closer Russo-Japanese relations will promote the domestic communist movement. (7) A Russo-Japanese-"Manchukuo" alliance may invite communist forces to invade "Manchukuo," which is unfavorable to Japan's policy.

Tokyo dispatch from the Domei News Agency, 24th: Prime Minister Saito expressed his opinion yesterday in Hayama that a Russo-Japanese non-aggression treaty could be concluded. The Foreign Ministry's leadership, based on the fundamental reasons that (1) the Soviet Russian government is in a position of non-responsibility regarding the Comintern, and even if a non-aggression treaty is concluded, the Soviet Russian government does not guarantee ideological aggression, and (1) there is no need for a general non-aggression treaty in the current Russo-Japanese relations, but what is needed is a concrete and friendly relationship in economic relations, believes that it is still too early to conclude a non-aggression treaty. However, it does not oppose a temporary and partial non-aggression treaty on the Kwantung Army side. Regarding the Sakhalin or Korean borders, similar to the existing military agreements between Japan and Russia, concluding a temporary and partial non-aggression treaty between Japan, Russia, and "Manchukuo," including "Manchukuo," seems more appropriate. However, it has not yet been decided whether the Japanese side will propose this. Currently, both the Foreign Ministry and the military are studying this.

Tokyo dispatch from the China United News Agency, 24th: The Japanese Ambassador to Russia, *

Hirota, was ordered to enter the palace at 2:00 PM today to give an *

account to the Emperor of the recent situation in Soviet Russia and Russia's policy towards Japan.

Navy Minister Okada Resigns Due to Age

General Ambo May Succeed Him

Tokyo dispatch from the China United News Agency, 24th: Navy Minister Okada will reach the naval retirement age next spring. It is rumored that Minister Okada has decided to retire from active duty and resign from the position of Navy Minister. The Navy plans to recommend General Ambo as his successor.

Tokyo dispatch from the Domei News Agency, 24th: Navy Minister Okada will reach the retirement age of 65 at the end of January next year. At that time, the Navy Minister will either retire as stipulated or remain in active duty by some other means. The military and various other sectors are paying close attention to this. It seems that the Navy Minister has resolved to clear the way for younger generations, mentally resign from the position of Minister, and retire from active duty. When the Saito Cabinet was established, the Prime Minister's earnest requests forced him to serve as Navy Minister for the second time. He intended to cleanly retire after tidying up the aftermath of the May 15 Incident, purifying the morale within the department, and completing the replenishment of military strength caused by the London Naval Treaty. Since then, the May 15 Incident has been handled step by step according to the Navy Minister's policy, and there is no longer any disturbance within the Navy Department. The purification within the department can be completed with the regular personnel changes in December to refresh the ranks and prepare for the future. Regarding the replenishment of military strength following the London Naval Treaty, it will be included in the second replenishment plan in the next fiscal year's budget and supplementary budget to supplement the shortcomings and renew the Navy. This is the Navy Minister's desired goal, which can be fully realized, so he plans to take the opportunity to retire bravely. However, Prime Minister Saito and the Navy's top leaders are concerned that Okada's brave retirement at this time will have a major impact.

Philippine Independence Issue

To Be Presented to the US Congress This Session for Discussion

Some Advocate Establishing a Neutral Country

To Ease Tensions Between the US and Japan

Washington dispatch from the National News Agency, 23rd: Today, it is widely rumored here that if the United States allows the Philippines complete independence and its sovereignty is guaranteed by a neutrality treaty, then many important figures in Japan will also support the same neutrality for Manchuria. It is said that foreign diplomats here have already secretly discussed the possibility of this neutrality movement, but no one is willing to publicly propose this plan. However, the diplomats participating in the discussion generally believe that if treaties of neutrality are concluded for both regions, it would open a way to resolve the urgent problems in the Far East. It is also heard that some leading figures in Japan especially favor concluding a treaty for the permanent neutrality of Manchuria, hoping to refute other countries' accusations that Japan wants to expand its territory. According to reports, the Philippine independence issue was initially just a matter of partisan disputes in the United States. The Republican Party opposed independence, while the Democratic Party favored independence under considerable guarantees. Since the economic depression, sugar-producing states and dairy farmers in the United States have been greatly afraid of competition from Philippine sugar and coconut oil, so even Republicans have supported independence. The House of Representatives in the last session had already passed a bill for independence after eight years. After the current Congress convenes, the Senate will also begin deliberations on this matter.

US Representative Meets British Prime Minister

Havas, 24th: London: Davis, the US representative attending the Disarmament Conference, was received by British Prime Minister MacDonald this morning to discuss everything and talk about the possibility of immediate implementation. Herriot Delivers a Somber Speech on a Former Battlefield

A Heartfelt Plea for Peace

Havas, 23rd: Lains: Lains is located in the plain of northern France, with the rolling hills of Lorette in between, which was the site of fierce battles between the two armies during the European War. Approximately one hundred thousand soldiers from the German and French armies are buried here. Prime Minister Herriot's speech yesterday was given at this old battlefield filled with grave mounds. Although the Prime Minister's speech was not political in nature, it inevitably concluded with an appeal to all nations to abandon past grievances and reconcile with each other. His speech, given in a place that had endured the suffering of war, made his appeal especially meaningful. Herriot then said that northern France, which had been devastated by war, with 2.5 million acres of land, had surprisingly been restored to its original state in ten years. The efforts of the French people are truly amazing. Herriot also said, "After the war, everything was desolate. However, workers and farmers worked tirelessly to bring life back to the vast land. Such immortal achievements are truly amazing. However, such efforts are beyond ordinary limits. If the people continue to do so, the nation will lose its life. What we see before us shows that the nations of the world should reconcile with each other." Herriot also said that peace cannot be achieved with empty words. He said, "The person speaking to you is a believer in upholding peace. He has come here to give his advice to all those who are sincere. Let us try to discard prejudices, broaden our horizons, and think calmly. Then we will know that the vast majority of the 75,000 German soldiers who lie buried here also wanted to enjoy the happiness of peace and work. What France hopes for is that all nations will abandon their grievances and join hands together. I said this in 1924. I hope that the people of all countries can take France as a model. The work of 1924 was continued by us in Geneva and Lausanne. Regarding material interests, France does not want to argue with others, so it only practices philanthropy. Therefore, France is planning to establish a plan to link disarmament and security with each other, and use the power of legal development to seek the abolition of armaments. The French government is tirelessly working on this cause. To be successful, all nations must be as rational as France."

British Newspaper Commentary

On the Status of Chinese Government Bonds

Reuters, 24th: London: The Times criticized the status of Chinese government bonds today, saying that the number of drawn bonds that have not been redeemed has increased year by year. In February of this year, the Stock Exchange Council allowed the trading of these bonds, considering them special transactions, and the Chinese government paid interest on both drawn and undrawn bonds when issuing back interest. From then on, the Chinese government will likely continue to do so. According to this situation, the market's claim that there is not much difference between drawn and undrawn Chinese bonds is not without reason. If drawn bonds are still not redeemed, then a strange situation will soon occur, that is, the number of drawn bonds will exceed the number of undrawn bonds.

Published

Havas, 23rd: London: The British Foreign Office notified the Soviet representative in London on October 17 that the temporary commercial agreement signed between the UK and the Soviet Union in London on April 16, 1930, is now terminated according to the provisions of Article 7, Section 1 of the agreement, effective April 17, 1933. The Mystery of the French Prime Minister's Visit to Spain

National News Agency, 23rd: Paris: Although official sources have made great efforts to deny the widely circulated rumor of a Franco-Spanish defense alliance regarding French Prime Minister Herriot's planned visit to Madrid, it does not seem to match the facts. According to reliable sources, even if Herriot's visit to Spain does not result in a Franco-Spanish defense alliance, there must be some other plan. This so-called other plan is a treaty established between France and Spain that, in the future, when France is at war, foreign colonial troops can be transported to the European continent and then transported north via Spanish railways to avoid the dangers of sea transport. Furthermore, Herriot intends to have Spain guarantee the strict neutrality of the Strait of Gibraltar to prevent the fortresses there from being seized by the Italian navy if France and Italy go to war in the future. France attaches great value to these conditions and is prepared to grant Spain important concessions in North Africa and provide it with substantial loans in economic terms.

British Newspapers Pay Close Attention to Matsuoka's Trip to Geneva

The government especially noted the remarks he made on the eve of his departure. His claim that he opposes the Lytton Report's recommendation that the sovereignty of the three northeastern provinces be returned to China has not been given much attention. The Daily News said that the longer the Lytton Report is studied, the more its proposals are seen as suitable for political maneuvering. Last year, the report almost granted Japan everything it asked for. Does Japan want an honorable solution, or does it want to be an enemy of the whole world? Japan is between these two. Even the militarists should allow Matsuoka to seek an honorable peace and end the entanglement that has not stopped.

Japan Participates in the Chicago Exposition

The Budget is Projected at 230,000 Yen

Japan United Press, 24th: Tokyo: The Ministry of Finance announced that the international exposition will be held in Chicago in June of next year. Japan has decided to participate in this exposition with a budget of 230,068 yen, which will be paid from the second reserve fund of the seventh year of Showa.

The Invention of the Underwater Tank

Havas, 23rd: Madrid: Spanish worker Ruiz invented an underwater tank and used electricity to separate pure water, separating light oxygen and hydrogen. He used oxygen for the people in the car to breathe. Today, Ruiz tested the car in the Cabo Lago in Cadiz. No fewer than 15,000 people watched around the lake. The car first circled the lake and then entered the water. Ruiz, sitting in the car, sent a message from the bottom of the lake praising the republic and the current government and expressing his respect to those who had caused misfortune at sea and were buried in the belly of the fish. The car lasted 95 minutes underwater. Later, the lake water gradually seeped into the car, and the car had to be lifted out of the water. It is said that Ruiz will continue to experiment.

Public Telegram

From Hailar: To the Shen Bao and the Anti-Japanese Support Association: It has been a year since the Northeast fell into enemy hands. However, our last piece of pure land on the Manchurian border has been supported with painstaking efforts, all thanks to our Garrison Commander Su Bingwen. Now, representatives from various regions and commanders of various volunteer armies have gathered in Hailar to plot national salvation. They have unanimously elected Commander Su as the commander-in-chief of the Northeast People's National Salvation Army. He took office on the first of this month and simultaneously telegraphed to announce to the people of the country that he would soon send troops to divide and advance, engage in fierce battles day after day, and repeatedly thwart the enemy's attacks. Recapturing Longjiang is within reach. The news has spread, and the people of the world are united. The people of the Northeast, especially, are deeply indignant. Even women and children in remote rural areas have saved food and clothing to support our soldiers. However, the Manchurian border is desolate, with a red land stretching for thousands of miles. After the war, the number of residents has decreased, and the usual military pay relies on relief. Now that we are facing a crisis of external resistance, we are even more afraid of running out of food and failing to accomplish our mission. The success or failure of our mission hangs in the balance. The need for assistance is urgent, like a spark igniting our hearts. We have long admired your newspaper's and association's compassion for the hungry and the drowning. You have long been known for your clear reputation of saving the people and the country. With great sincerity, we send this telegram to implore you to provide rice and other aid. We rely on your advocacy. If you can give a high call, it will surely resonate across the mountains. Providing a continuous supply and mobilizing the people will ensure that the righteous army has no worries about food and can successfully save the country. Our eagerness to hear from you is pressing. We are sending the funds directly to the American firm, Shin Shen Company, in Hailar. Please send a receipt to show good faith. We have also heard that the Ji Lu County People's National Salvation Support Association in Heilongjiang Province is knocking at your door.

Important News

Tianjin Tram Workers' Strike

Party and Government Agencies are Mediating

Tianjin Communication: The Tianjin Tram and Electric Light Company was founded in 1904 (the 30th year of the reign of Emperor Guangxu of the Qing Dynasty) by the Belgian firm, Seichang & Co., when Yuan Shikai was the Minister of Beiyang. It has been 28 years since then. Now, due to the rapid expansion of business, the annual profit is around 3 million. In recent years, labor disputes have arisen from time to time due to the poor treatment of workers. This spring, when tram fares were raised, the entire city opposed it, and there were already signs of a tram workers' strike. Later, because the workers accepted advice from all sides that workers must jointly maintain local order during a period of serious national crisis, the tram workers' union postponed the strike. On the 14th of this month, the workers, citing the fact that the company had not only failed to sign the eight demands it had promised in March of last year, but also had not fully implemented them, convened a temporary workers' representative conference and resolved to submit seven more demands to the company. The demands are: 1. All company employees should be issued two seasons of official clothing each year. 2. Those who die while in the service of the company due to illness should be given a funeral allowance of 200 yuan per person (those who die on duty are not included). 3. Employees who are in the service of the company should be provided with official housing by the company. If there is no official housing, each person should be given a housing allowance of 3 yuan. 4. Employees who are in the service of the company should be provided with free electricity up to 20 kWh per month. Those who exceed 20 kWh should be charged at a rate of 12 cents per kWh. 5. The Inspection Department should continue to provide a bonus of 3 yuan per month to those who work hard on public affairs. 6. Reading boards should be set up at appropriate locations in the Machinery Department, the Power Plant, and the Electric Light Department. 7. The monthly subsidy for the workers' children's school should be increased by 100 yuan. After the resolutions were made, the union reported the conditions to the Party and government authorities and requested them to mediate in order to achieve a peaceful solution. The Social Affairs Bureau sent personnel to contact the company, but the company refused to accept them, saying that the newly appointed general manager was about to arrive in China from Belgium and the old general manager was not responsible for handling the union's affairs. Upon hearing this, the union convened a joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees on the evening of the 20th. The masses were outraged and decided to go on strike uniformly starting on the morning of yesterday (the 21st) to urge the company to come to its senses. For the past two days, all tram passengers have not had to purchase tickets. As a result, men, women, old and young, who usually walked instead of taking the tram, have all been taking the tram, resulting in an unusual number of passengers. The speed of the tram has also been slowed down due to passengers rushing on and off. The order of the city has been slightly affected, but fortunately, no accidents have occurred, and public security has not been affected. Except for the workers in the power plant, who are still working, and all the workers repairing the street lights, the electric light department has gone on strike. The street lights are not turned off even during the day in order to consume electricity. The company's attitude has become even tougher as the workers have gone on strike. The Belgian consul has also contacted our authorities yesterday. The Belgian manager, Wang Kesen, went to the provincial government this morning to see Chairman Yu and asked him to stop the strike. The outcome is still unknown. However, Chairman Yu told reporters that he had not heard of the strike before it occurred. Although the company recognizes the provincial government as the negotiating counterpart, it had not reported to the government beforehand. He has now handed the matter over to the municipal government for prompt handling. The municipal government has instructed the Social Affairs Bureau and the Public Security Bureau to mediate properly. The Civil Affairs Section Director Yang Litan of the Municipal Party Committee has also gone with government personnel to handle the matter. However, at present, the attitudes of both parties are tough, making mediation difficult. The company's losses are close to 10,000 yuan per day. If the delay continues, the losses will be even greater. (October 22)

Central Party Headquarters Memorial Week 6

Ding Chao-wu Reports on Saving the Nation and Eradicating Humiliation

The Central Committee held its weekly memorial service for the late Premier at 9 a.m. on the 24th. Those in attendance included Central Committee members Chen Guofu, Chu Minyi, Ding Chao-wu, Chen Lifu, Zeng Kuoqing, Li Ciwen, Xie Zuomin, Chen Zhaoying, Xiao Zhongzhen, Huang Jichen, Zheng Zhannan, Hong Ludong, Miao Peicheng, and over six hundred staff members. Chairman Chen Guofu presided, and Ding Chao-wu delivered a report titled "Saving the Nation and Eradicating Humiliation," which roughly stated: Faced with the pressing threat from foreign powers, everyone should prepare "how to save the nation and eradicate humiliation," learn from Goujian's decade of recuperation and education, and strive to strengthen our power. The Chinese people often suffer rudeness and contempt from foreigners, experiencing no small amount of insult and stimulation, yet they remain immersed in a life of pleasure and do not consider it shameful. Therefore, the first step is to awaken the public to "know shame." Next, focus on recuperation and education to cultivate a weak nation. Furthermore, gather human and material resources, unite and consolidate. The Party should unite the people with sincerity, using the Premier's methods, and employ self-governance to seek unity, so that the power to resist foreign aggression will naturally arise. The "Method of Implementing Currency Revolution," "Methods for Promoting Cooperatives," and "Methods for Regulating Food Supply," recently proposed by Mr. Chen Guofu, are indeed excellent plans for saving the nation if implemented. Finally, it is necessary to train the people to develop good habits of observing order and knowing etiquette, promote the spirit of martial valor, and eliminate weak and useless phenomena, then the future will naturally have hope. After the report, the meeting adjourned.

The Land Tax Assessment Crisis in Jiangdu Becomes More Serious 7

Tens of Thousands of Villagers Gather, Clashing with Military Police

Military Police Open Fire, Killing Seven Villagers and Wounding Over Ten

Traffic Disrupted, City Gates Closed, Shops Also Shut Down

Yangzhou Correspondence: The second wave of land tax assessment turmoil in the Second District of Jiangdu is expanding. After the county government was destroyed last night (the 22nd), military police arrested 250 villagers, both men and women, in separate operations. County Magistrate Yang held court overnight, interrogating them until dawn. According to Magistrate Yang, although the villagers are not suspected of being incited by communists, there are local bullies instigating them from within. However, the villagers continued to sound gongs throughout the night, and the turmoil spread further. This morning (the 23rd), over ten thousand men and women gathered at the Fuyun Gate, Xu Ning Gate, and the opposite bank of the river, each holding farm implements and other items, preventing the passage of boats. By noon, even cars could not pass. Many shops in the city remained closed. Military, political, and police agencies received information in advance and dispatched teams to the city to prevent and closely monitor the situation. The scene of officials and civilians confronting each other across the river was more serious than yesterday. The villagers in the Fuyun Gate area were particularly numerous, occupying civilian boats and ferries, surging across the river to confront the military police, resulting in a conflict. As a result, the military police opened fire, killing Xu Xueqing (resident of San Cha He), Mao Anlong, Xie Chunrong (resident of Kong Jia Zhuang), Yin Yu Shi (resident of Shi Jia Qiao Yang Jia Zhuang), Yin Xu Shi (resident of Jiang Yin Jia Zhuang), Huang Gui Shi (resident of Zhuan Qiao), Lu Yuzhen (resident of Xin He Wan), and seven other men and women on the spot. Zhu Da Liang's wife, Zhu Xiao Guniang (Guan Yin Xiang), Xie Yong'an (resident of Shui Long Qiao), Jiang Da (resident of Han Jia Zhuang), a Kong (resident of Dai Jia Zhuang), Yang Dai Shi (resident of Yang Jia Zhuang), Zhu Li Shi (resident of Yan Jia Xiang), Zhou Hongtao (resident of Xue Jia Lou), Jin Yin Shi, Huang Shi (resident of Yang Jia Qiao), and over ten other men and women were wounded. Seeing that many were killed and injured, the villagers retreated in fear. The military police immediately entered the city and closed the city gates. At the same time, villagers strongly desired to enter the city through other gates, so those gates were also closed. By about 10 a.m., traffic in and out of the city was completely cut off, and cars and boats stopped running. After the city gates were closed, the military police were armed and on alert on the city walls. The villagers could not enter the city and only cried outside the city. Later, the Second Battalion of the Independent Regiment and the Provincial Security Team successively came out of the city to suppress the situation, and order was slightly restored. The wounded villagers were carried to the home of Wang Jingting, chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, to be treated (Wang's house is located at the earth dam outside the South Gate). Wang's residence then contacted various chambers of commerce by phone to request doctors to go out of the city for treatment. The county party headquarters, considering that this turmoil was expanding, invited Central Committee member Wang Boling, as well as heads of military, political, and police agencies, and leaders of various legal entities to a meeting this morning to discuss solutions. Wang Boling immediately stated that while the suffering of the people should be considered, the authority of the government should also be maintained. The government might accept the legitimate demands of the people. He immediately nominated Standing Committee Member Yu of the County Party Headquarters, Executive Committee Member Lin, Chairman Wang of the Chamber of Commerce, and Director Shi of the Farmers' Association, a total of four people, to be led by Commander Li out of the city to solicit the opinions of the villagers. The representatives departed at about 12 o'clock, first going to the East Gate to climb the city wall and announce that the villagers should retreat to the side of the Dutian Temple in the east of the river to wait for the discussion. The villagers agreed. The representatives left the city, crossed the river to that location, and Wang Jingting announced that everything should be proposed by the villagers in two points: first, all those arrested should be released; second, there should be no further investigation of farmland. The representatives also went to the bus station and announced that the villagers also demanded the same as before. The representatives answered regarding the first point that as long as the villagers no longer took actions outside of the law, the administrative side could release those arrested. Regarding the second point, it was necessary to follow proper procedures and jointly negotiate a solution with representatives publicly elected by the villagers. The villagers indicated their acceptance and then nominated more than ten representatives. Wang Jingting and others entered the city with them and went to the County Party Headquarters to request that Central Committee member Wang, County Magistrate Yang, and Commander Li come to the headquarters for consultation. It is reported that County Magistrate Yang has agreed that the arrested villagers can be released separately tomorrow after providing guarantees. It is reported that the county government has already telegraphed the circumstances of the incident to the provincial government yesterday and has received a reply from the provincial government today. The general idea is that the villagers' riot is indeed reprehensible, but the county magistrate's handling was also improper and that he should quickly consider and arrange for a settlement of the aftermath and not allow the turmoil to expand. Chairman Gu also telegraphed Commander Li to assist in maintaining order. The Finance Department also sent Wang Luzhi and the Provincial Security Office sent Yin Xingru to Yangzhou yesterday to secretly investigate the truth of the turmoil. Because land and water traffic between Zhenjiang and Yangzhou was cut off this afternoon, the provincial government telegraphed Bureau Chief Chen of the Public Security Bureau to inquire about the situation. The injured villagers have been sent to hospitals in the city and Zhenjiang for treatment. The bodies of those killed are still lying outside the Fuyun Gate, and their families are holding their bodies and crying in grief. Tonight, the city is under special martial law, and traffic is cut off at 8 p.m., prohibiting pedestrians from passing. It is reported that at about 11 o'clock, the villagers retreated to the area outside the East Gate and continued to sound gongs, and many boats were seized. (Night of the 23rd)

Jiangsu Provincial Government 8

Orders All Counties to Temporarily Suspend Land Tax Assessments

The Jiangsu Provincial Government believes that the expedient method of rectifying land tax is related to the land reclamation plan proposed by the Land Bureau, and its implementation should be temporarily suspended in order to solve the problem comprehensively. It was proposed at the 536th meeting and resolved to be handed over to the Civil Affairs and Finance Departments for consultation, and then submitted for approval before proceeding. Yesterday (the 23rd), the provincial government issued an order to all counties to comply. The original order is recorded as follows: "According to Item 7 of the matters discussed at the 563rd meeting of the Provincial Government Committee, the chairman proposed that the method of rectifying land tax to be submitted by the Finance Department and the land reclamation plan proposed by the Land Bureau, which is currently under review, although there is a difference between expedient and fundamental measures, there is a suspicion of duplication in the procedures. How should it be handled to clarify powers and benefit administration? Please review and make a public resolution. The resolution was that the method of rectifying land tax is related to the land reclamation plan proposed by the Land Bureau. It will be handed over to the Civil Affairs and Finance Departments for consultation, and then submitted for approval before proceeding. The order is for all counties to comply and to inform the two departments, etc. Recorded. In addition to ordering the Civil Affairs and Finance Departments to review and separately distribute the order, the county magistrate is hereby ordered to obey and comply."

Inauguration of the Kalachakra Mandala Ceremony in Beiping 9

Approximately 100,000 Attendees

Initiation Ceremony Held in the Afternoon

Beiping Correspondence: Kalachakra Mandala Ceremony for Calamity Relief and Salvation

Page 8

Starting from 6:30 AM today, the ceremony was inaugurated at the Hall of Supreme Harmony. Military and political dignitaries from Beiping and Tianjin, prominent figures from the opposition, people from all walks of life, Mongolian princes, commoners, and Lamaist monks attended, reaching 100,000 participants, truly a unprecedented grand event in Beiping. The situation during the ceremony is recorded below:

Arrangement of the Venue: Elaborate colorful archways were erected at the Meridian Gate and the East and West Flowery Gates. Participants entered with tickets. National flags and various dharma flags were hung at the Gate of Supreme Harmony. Inside the gate, the ground of the Danbi courtyard was covered with palm mats and reed mats. Those without altar passes were restricted to this area, sitting on the mats. Attendees with altar passes gathered on the dais in the hall, approximately 2,000 people. The platform was covered with red carpet, and the audience sat on the ground. The left side was for lamas and Mongolians, and the right side was for people from all walks of life, mostly women and the elderly. Many wore Western suits and leather shoes.

In the center of the hall in front of the platform, a Dharma altar was set up, about ten feet high. The altar was covered with red silk, and the dharma table was wrapped in yellow satin. Dharma instruments were placed on the table, and a wooden ladder was placed next to the altar. The left side of the altar was for the seats of Mongolian princes and military and political leaders, and the right side was for foreign guests. Many Mongolian princes and military and political dignitaries were not seated, but rested inside the hall. The foreign guest area was full.

In front of the guest seats in the Hall of Supreme Harmony, a special Buddha seat was set up for the Panchen Lama. The center of the hall was surrounded by yellow ropes to create a restricted area. On the left were offerings of fruits, rice, and sugar arranged on tables. On the right was the mandala, an octagonal shape made of yellow silk. Brocade banners were hung on the city. The pavilion in the center of the city was also colored in red and yellow. Eight Buddha tables were placed on the eight sides of the city, each with copper plates, oil lamps, and pots and bottles of dharma instruments.

Initiation Ceremony: The chanting of scriptures began at 6:30 AM and ended at 12:00 PM. The initiation ceremony was held from 2:00 PM. At 2:00 PM, the audience took their seats. At 2:15 PM, the lamas began to play music. At 2:20 PM, the Panchen Lama came out of the hall and ascended to the seat. The Panchen Lama wore a yellow dharma robe, a red shawl on his left shoulder, his right arm bare, holding a copper bell, and sat in meditation with crossed legs. At this time, the audience below the stage prostrated and paid homage. After a while, the Panchen Lama held pink scriptures and began to lecture. His speech was very fast and he coughed frequently. After finishing one volume, the Khenpo translated it into Chinese. The lecture lasted about an hour, and the audience presented hadas to the Panchen Lama. For a moment, yellow and blue silk scarves piled up several feet high. The Panchen Lama also sent his disciples to distribute saffron holy water and five-colored rice flowers to the audience.

Shortly after, the initiation ceremony continued. First, his disciples used copper cups to anoint the foreheads and chins of the audience with holy oil. The Panchen Lama also personally performed the initiation for military and political dignitaries. The first to receive the initiation were Zhang Xueliang, followed by Duan Qirui, Zhu Qinglan, Wu Guangxin, Cao Rulin, and Wang Yitang. After the initiation, Tibetan grass and red ropes were distributed. The audience on the altar scrambled to seize them from the lamas, but the audience below the stage received nothing.

After a while, Mongolians brought grass down from the altar and scattered it, causing the audience to crowd and struggle for it. After a long time, they managed to escape. After the red ropes and Tibetan grass were distributed, the Panchen Lama continued to lecture until 5:00 PM when he stepped down. The first day of the assembly ended. (October 21st)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang Province Orders Examination of Primary School Teachers: The Education Department of Jiangsu Province Has Conducted Several Examinations and Certifications of Primary School Teachers in the Past. The Education Department Believes That Examination and Certification is the Best Way to Alleviate the Current Shortage of Teachers, Carefully Select Talent, and Promote Education. Upon Investigation, Many Primary School Teachers in Various Counties Are Unqualified and Fill Positions Improperly. Those Teachers Who Should Be Tested Often Avoid the Examination on Various Pretexts, Which Goes Against the Principle of Carefully Selecting Teachers. It Is Now Scheduled That the Fourth Examination and Certification of Primary School Teachers Will Be Held from April 3rd to 5th of Next Year. Registration Will Begin Immediately and End on January 31st of Next Year. The Original Registration Fee Was One Yuan, but in Consideration of Financial Difficulties, It Has Been Reduced to Fifty Cents. The Education Bureau of This County Has Complied with the Order and Issued a Notice. Wuxi

The Issue of District Secretaries Creates a Stalemate: Since Receiving the Order to Organize the Collection Office, the County Finance Bureau Appointed Lu Dingxin as Director. It Was Officially Established Last Month. It Instructed the District Secretaries of Each Ward to Submit Household Registers to the Bureau. The Transfer of Real Estate Is Now Under the Jurisdiction of the Collection Office. There Are a Total of 416 Wards in the County, with 416 District Secretaries. If They Are All Dismissed, Their Livelihoods Will Be Cut Off. Therefore, They Jointly Sent Representatives to Petition Director Wang, Requesting That They Be Changed to Collection Staff According to the Dongtai Method. Director Wang Replied That He Had Not Received a Clear Order from His Superiors, So There Has Been No Result. The Issue Has Been Delayed Until Now. The Second Installment of Land Tax Is About to Be Collected, and Official Books Need to Be Prepared Urgently. Both Sides Are Disputing the Matter, So the Preparation of Books Has Not Yet Begun. The Books Will Not Be Prepared If the Issue Is Not Resolved One Day. This Has Created a Stalemate.

The Agricultural Bank Handles Relief for Farmers by Accepting Rice as Collateral: Wuxi Agricultural Bank, in Order to Regulate Farmers' Grain and Support the Rural Economy, Is Holding Rice Collateral at the Beginning of the New Grain Season. This Year, Rice Prices Are Low, and Farmers Are in Great Difficulty. Therefore, the Bank Has Decided to Accept Grain Collateral Within Its Capacity, First in Dongting, Nanqiao Temple Head, Qianqiao, and Four Other Locations, with a Total Amount of 20,000 to 30,000 Piculs. The Collateral Will Be Limited to White Rice. The Collateral Price Will Be 70% to 80% of the Market Price. The Collateral Will Begin in Early December. As for the Issue of Grain Relief in All Areas of the County, the Entire Plan of Organizing or Promoting the Organization of Public Warehouses to Receive Farmers' Collateral Is Under the Responsibility of the Competent Authorities. The Agricultural Bank Will Not Intervene.

Changshu

A Suspicious Murder Case Was Re-Examined in Zhenru: The Case of Xu Zhao, a Peasant Woman From Tiangzhuang, Changshu, Who Died Unexplained, Was Reported to the County by Local Citizens Yang Qiyu and Yang Zhenmin. They Said That After Xu Died, She Fell Into the River and Had Wounds on Her Body. The Local County Government Then Requested the Higher Court to Send Forensic Official Xuan Fang to Changshu. On September 18th, He Performed a Bone Steaming Examination Outside the North Gate. The Result Showed No Wounds. Xuan Concluded That She Had Fallen Into the River and Died Before Her Death. The Two Informants, Yang, Were Arrested. Yang Refused to Accept This and Appealed to the High Court for a Re-Examination. The High Court Approved and Designated the Zhenru Forensic Medicine Research Institute to Conduct the Examination Yesterday (the 24th) in Zhenru. The Original Informants and the Corpse's Family Arrived in Zhenru the Day Before. The Corpse's Bones Were Carefully Packed in a Box and Sent by Clerk Zhang Accompanied by Bailiffs. At 9:30 AM Yesterday, the Director of the Forensic Medicine Research Institute, Lin Ji, Briefly Questioned the Plaintiff and Defendant Before Entering the Morgue to Examine Xu Zhao's Bones. The Examination Found That There Was Mud and Sand in the Corpse's Bones' Nails, and There Was Also a Lot of Yellow Sand Mixed in the Brain Matter, Making It Difficult to Examine. However, It Was Observed That the Deceased Fell Into the River Before Death. The Skull and Frontal Bone Had Cracks and Bloodstains, Proving That She Died of Suffocation. There Was a Black Spot on the Right Hip Bone, Indicating That She Had Been Injured, But It Was Difficult to Determine Whether It Was a Fall or a Beating. As for the Other Injuries, They Were Probably Skin and Flesh Injuries. Most of the Bones Had Been Damaged During the First Bone Steaming and Were Difficult to Examine. A Detailed Expert Report Will Be Issued Within a Week After Further Examination. The Corpse's Family and the Original Informants Were Taken Back to Kunshan by the Bailiffs and Were Scheduled to Return to Changshu Today to Report Back.

Weng Zhaoyuan Came to Hangzhou to Visit the Aviation School: Weng Zhaoyuan, the Commander of the 156th Brigade of the 19th Route Army, Fought Heroically Against the Japanese in Wusong During the Shanghai War and Won the Sympathy and Support of the People of the Country. They Then Rode in a Car Into the City to Discuss Aviation and the Overall Development Plan. It Is Said That Weng Will Stay in Hangzhou for a Few More Days.

A Boiler Explosion in a Factory Killed and Injured Many People: At 3:00 PM Today (the 24th), at the Machine Factory on the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway at Jianggan Gate, a Boiler Suddenly Exploded Due to Excessive Steam Pressure. A Western-Style House Was Completely Destroyed. Four Workers, Wang Changming, Shen Jinchun, Zhao Ayou, and Shan Mingde, Were Killed Instantly. Their Bodies Were Scattered, and the Scene Was Very Tragic. Four People Were Seriously Injured, Including Zeng Ji and Chen Yantang. Two People Were Slightly Injured, Tong Yongjin and Others. The Colleagues in the Factory Were All in Tears at the Sight and Immediately Carried the Injured to the Jiangshu Che and Took Them to Guangji Hospital in the City for Treatment. However, Chen Yantang Was Too Seriously Injured to Be Saved and Died in the Hospital. Zeng Ji and the Other Three Were Also Scalded All Over and Were in Critical Condition.

Taizhou

Bandits in Wen Belonging Were Defeated: Zhang Zhuqing, a Notorious Bandit in Wenyi, Gathered Hundreds of Followers and Set Fire to and Looted in Wen and Huang Counties. He Had Been Ordered to Be Arrested Many Times, but He Had Not Been Caught. He Is Now Gathered at Daoshi Guanhaishan in Wenyi. This Was Discovered by Xu Menggao, the Battalion Commander of the Third Battalion of the Fifth Regiment of the Zhejiang Provincial Security Team Stationed in Wenyi. He Specially Coordinated With the Taian Gunboat Stationed in Jiao (Haimen, Under the Jurisdiction of Taizhou) and Led a Large Force to Suppress Them. The Bandits Dared to Resist and Engaged in a Fierce Battle for a Day and Night. The Bandits Were Unable to Withstand the Attack and Fled in Disarray. More Than Thirty Bandits Were Killed on the Spot, Four Were Captured Alive, and Dozens of Guns Were Seized. This Has Been Reported to the Fifth Regiment Headquarters Stationed in Jiao for the Record. The Lu Jiao Bus Had an Accident: The Bus From Luqiao to Linhai Haimen Drove From Luqiao to Jipaitou at 5:00 PM the Day Before Yesterday. In Order to Avoid Pedestrians, the Bus Drove Horizontally Into the Field, Crushing Passenger Wang Xianyou to Death and Injuring Twelve People, With a Loss of More Than 1,000 Yuan.

Education News

Important News

Three Orders From the Ministry of Education

Reduce Tuition Fees for Students From Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang

Investigate the Statistics of Overseas Chinese Schools

Order to Report Administrative Personnel Expenses in Each Province

Nanjing, 24th Telegram: The Ministry of Education Issued an Order to the Education Departments and Bureaus of Each Province and City, Saying: Since the Northeast Incident Occurred, the Families of Students From Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang Provinces Have Had Difficulty With Financial Support. Students Enrolled in Public and Private Universities and Colleges Have Been Ordered by the Ministry to Appropriately Reduce or Exempt Their Tuition Fees for This Semester. Now, If There Are Any New Students From These Provinces in Provincial and Registered Private Vocational Schools, They Should Be Allowed to Appropriately Reduce or Exempt Their Tuition Fees for This Semester to Provide Relief.

The Ministry of Education Issued an Order to Overseas Chinese Schools in Various Consulates Abroad, Saying: The Ministry Previously Issued an Investigation Form. However, the Reports Were Not Complete, and There Are Still No Statistics on Overseas Chinese Schools. Now, One Copy Each of the Statistical Forms for Secondary Schools and Elementary Education in the 19th and 20th Years Are Sent. Please Distribute Them to the Overseas Chinese Secondary and Elementary Schools in Your Area and Have Them Filled Out and Submitted to the Ministry Within One Month of Receiving the Order. Do Not Delay or Omit Any Information.

In Order to Investigate the Statistics of National Education Administrative Expenses and Provincial Education Administrative Personnel, the Ministry of Education Issued an Order to the Education Departments and Bureaus of Each Province and City to Prepare and Submit Them Within Ten Days. Do Not Delay.

The Fujian Education Department Set Up Scholarship Funds

Ten People Will Be Selected at the Beginning of the Winter Vacation

Fuzhou Correspondence: Cheng Shizhui, the Director of the Fujian Education Department, in Order to Assist Outstanding High School Graduates From Poor Families in the Province to Enter University, Has Set Up Scholarships for Poor Students. The Number of Scholarships Is Provisionally Set at Fifty, With Each Student Receiving a Scholarship of 300 Yuan Per Year (200 Yuan for Those in Provincial Universities) Until They Graduate From University. Starting From the 21st Year, It Was Originally Scheduled to Select Twenty People in the First Year. However, Since the Provisional Regulations for Scholarships Have Only Now Been Received by the Ministry and Approved for the Record, the Preparations Have Not Been Completed. It Is Now Scheduled to Select Ten People at the Beginning of the Winter Vacation. The Remaining Ten People Will Be Combined With the Selection in the Summer Vacation of the 22nd Year. It Is Reported That the Application Period for This Year's Selection Has Been Set From November 1st to November 30th. The Review Period Will Be From December 1st to January 20th. The Examination Will Be Held at the Education Department From January 20th to January 25th of the 22nd Year. A Selection Committee Will Also Be Organized. In Addition to the Director of the Department Serving as the Chairman of the Committee According to the Regulations, Six Other Committee Members Have Also Been Appointed: Zhong Dao of the Department Secretariat, Wei, Zheng Qinde of the Zhang Section, Tang Shouqian, Supervisor Ye Songpo, and Instructor Cheng Yuancheng.

City Education Association

The First Meeting of the Board of Directors and Supervisors

Huang Zaoxiong and Others as Executive Directors

Wu Kaixian Was Elected as Executive Supervisor

And Passed the Declaration of Establishment of the General Assembly

The First Meeting of the Board of Directors and Supervisors of the City Education Association Was Held Yesterday Afternoon at 3:00 PM in the Conference Room of the City Education Bureau. Executive Directors and Supervisors Were Elected, the Declaration of the General Assembly Was Passed, and Many Important Cases Were Discussed and Resolved. The Details of the Meeting Are Recorded Below:

The Board of Directors Meeting Was Attended by Directors Hao Naiding, Zheng Hongnian, Huang Zaoxiong, Chen Jicheng, Zhang Zhongdao, Zhang Zaibo, Ma Jiazhen, Zhou Feicheng, Xu Yiyu, Wu Xiu, and Mao Yun. Alternate Directors Zhou Darong, Wang Dechang, and Wang Yongzhi Were Also Present. Huang Zaoxiong Served as Chairman, and Ma Jiazhen Served as Recorder. After the Opening Ceremony, the Chairman Reported (Omitted). Then, the Following Motions Were Discussed: 1. Motion to Elect Three Executive Directors. It Was Resolved That Huang Zaoxiong, Zhou Feicheng, and Zhang Zhongdao Were Elected as Executive Directors. 2. How Should the Organizational Regulations and Rules of Procedure of This Association Be Drafted? It Was Resolved That the Executive Directors Should Draft Them and Submit Them to the Next Board of Directors Meeting for Discussion. 3. How Should the Location of This Association Be Determined? It Was Resolved That Wenzhi Road Should Be Temporarily Borrowed as the Temporary Location. 4. How Should the Regular Meeting Dates of This Association Be Determined? It Was Resolved That the Board of Directors Meeting Should Be Held Every Wednesday Afternoon at 4:00 PM. 5. Motion to Approve the Declaration of Establishment of This Association. It Was Resolved That the Amendment Be Approved. The Remaining Motions Are Omitted.

The Supervisors Meeting Was Attended by Supervisors Cheng Kuanzheng, Zhang Xiaotian, Wu Renqi, Zheng Tan, Du Gang, and Chen Bai. Cheng Kuanzheng Served as Chairman, and Du Gang Served as Recorder. After the Opening Ceremony, the Following Items Were Discussed: 1. How to Generate Executive Supervisors? It Was Resolved That Wu Kaixian Was Elected as Executive Director. 2. To Stipulate the Date of the Regular Meeting of the Association It Was Resolved That a Meeting Should Be Convened Once Every Two Months on the 15th of the Month. 3. It Was Proposed to Designate the Board Member to Formulate the Rules of Procedures It Was Resolved That the Executive Supervisors Draft Them. 4. The Declaration of Establishment of This Association Had Been Drafted and Submitted for Approval. It Was Resolved That the Amendment Be Approved.

Declaration of Establishment: Those Who Lavishly Discuss Education Today Mostly Advocate Empty Talk and Do Not Engage in Practical Work. Since the Founding of the Republic of China, Twenty-One Years Have Passed. Among Them, More Than Ten Years Have Been Spent on the Push and Remnants of Warlords. National Education Is on the Verge of Bankruptcy. The Educational Policies That Adapt to the Trends of the Times and Social Needs Have Not Been Determined. At the Same Time, Due to the Instability in the Country, National Education Cannot Achieve Uniformity and Prosperity. After the National Government Established Its Capital in Nanjing and Unified the Country, It Promulgated the Three Principles of the People as the Purpose of National Education. The Whole Country Has Something to Follow. If We Can Actively Implement It, We May Not Be Able to Achieve Considerable Results. Because of the Frequent Civil Wars and the Depleted Economy, Coupled With the Frequent Educational Trends, the Education of One Line of Life Is Not as Good as Extinguished. It Is Really Gratifying That Shanghai Is the First City in Asia. Business Is Prosperous, Industry Is Developed, and the Population Is More Than Three Million. The Tide of the East and West Cultures Take This as the Center of Contact and Stimulation. The Concentration of Talents and the Establishment of Schools in the Field of Education Cannot Be Compared With Any Other City in the Country. According to the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau's Investigation in the Second Semester of the Nineteenth Year, There Are 744 Elementary Schools, 125 Secondary Schools, and 33 Higher Schools. The Statistics Show That There Are 932 Schools, With Assets Reaching More Than 32 Million Yuan and Annual Revenue Reaching More Than 11 Million Yuan. Other Social Education and Cultural Institutions Are Not Included. Therefore, We Can See That the Educational Power in Shanghai Alone Is Strong. Shanghai Should Take the Lead in the Country in Promoting Academics and Transforming Customs. If We Compare and Study the Number of Public and Private Schools at All Levels in Shanghai, We Can Get a Good Impression. Why Has National Education Fallen Into Bankruptcy in the Past Ten Years? Because Educational Funding Has Not Been Guaranteed, the Expenses of Independent Military Needs Are Huge, and They Often Involve Educational Expenses. Strikes and Teachings Occur From Time to Time, Which Deeply Affects the Future of Education. This Is Not the Case in Shanghai. Except for Patriotic Movements or Other Movements, There Are Fewer Cases of Strikes and Teachings Caused Purely by Economic Relations. The Proportion of the Number of Private Schools to Public Schools in the City Is As Follows: Private Schools Account for 74% of Elementary Schools, While Public Schools Account for Only 26%. Private Schools Account for 90% of Secondary Schools, While Public Schools Account for Only 10%. Private Schools Account for 73% of Higher Schools, While Public Schools Account for Only 27%. Private Funding Is Generally the Responsibility of Private Groups and Is Not Affected by Political Trends. Among Those Who Run Education, There Must Be No Lack of Those Who Focus on Education As a Lifelong Career. Therefore, Although National Education Is in a State of Destruction and Fragmentation, the Education of Shanghai Alone Can Still Develop Year by Year and Maintain a Lifeline for National Education. Although Shanghai Has the Above-Mentioned Advantages, We Still Cannot Be Satisfied. In Terms of Higher Education, Most of Them Create Empty and Useless Talents That Cannot Meet the Needs of Modern China. In Terms of Primary and Secondary Education, The Administration Is Not Necessary for Improving. Since the January 28th Incident, the Unprecedented Calamities Suffered by Our Educational Circles in Shanghai Have Made Us Feel Deep Sadness. For Example, the Oriental Library, Which Treasures More Than 372,000 Volumes of Chinese and Foreign Books, Is the Most Complete Private Library in the Country. It Was Burned to Ashes by the Japanese Army. The Number of Schools Destroyed by the Ruthless Artillery Fire in the War Zone Is Countless. The Statistics Show That the Loss Is No Less Than Tens of Millions. The Only Remaining Cultural Institutions Have Been Brutally Trampled by the Japanese. From Now On, How Should We Work Hard to Revitalize Shanghai Education? How Should We Learn From the Past and Improve Shanghai Education? Creating Life for Shanghai Education Is to Save Fate for National Education. We Are All Part of the Educational Community. We Are All Responsible.

The Preparations for This Association Have Been Going on for a Year. Now, It Has Been Established. It Is an Honor to Be Entrusted by the Educational Circles in Shanghai. In Addition to Concentrating on Research to Promote Academics, It Has the Obligation to Assist and Promote the Government. Through Careful Research and Common Discussion, We Know That University Education Is In Vain and Impractical. Therefore, Higher Education Economics Needs to Be Concentrated, and Course Standards Need to Be Improved. As for Primary and Secondary Education, Many of Its Facilities Are Highly Corresponding to the Actual Life of the People. Elementary and Junior High Schools Lack Suitable Production Training, and Senior High Schools Are Mostly General Subjects. As a Result, Most Junior and High School Graduates Who Cannot Afford to Attend School Are Difficult to Find a Way Out. Therefore, Vocational Training in Primary and Secondary Schools Needs to Be Rescued. When the Current Political Training Period Also Encountered National Disasters, If We Want to Train the People, We Should Pay Attention to Popularizing People's Wisdom and Awakening the People's Consciousness. More Than Half of the School-Age Children in Shanghai Have Not Yet Enrolled in School. Therefore, the Popularization of Compulsory Education Is Imminent. Many Enthusiastic People in Shanghai Often Donate Money to Establish Schools. Private Schools Need to Be Encouraged by the Education Authorities. There Are Not Many Public Primary and Secondary Schools. Most of the Rest Are Private. Therefore, the Tuition Fees Charged Are Naturally Relatively High, Which Makes It Difficult for Poor Children to Afford School. How Should We Find a Way to Relief Them? At the Very Least, We Must Ensure That the Opportunity to Receive Compulsory Education Is Equal. Shanghai's Industry and Commerce Are Developed, and Factories Are Abundant. The Number of Laboring Classes Who Work Hard Reaches More Than 800,000. Most of These People Come From Rural Areas and Rarely Receive Education. Therefore, the Supplementary Education for Workers Should Be Carefully Planned and Provided for in a Comprehensive Manner. We Must Ensure That All Workers in the City Have the Opportunity to Study. There Are Only More Than Ten Libraries in Such a Large City With a Population of More Than Three Million That Are Related to Social Education. Among Them, In Addition to the Oriental Being Destroyed, Most of the Rest Are Only Simple Equipment. In Addition, Public Schools, Public Education Centers, and Public Sports Fields Are Rare. Museums Are Still Vacant. In the Future, If We Want to Improve the People's Knowledge, All Social Education Institutions Need to Be Expanded. Since the Shanghai War, Colleagues Have Deeply Felt the Lack of Practical Science in Our Country. Therefore, All Research and Inventions of Practical Science Need to Be Encouraged by the Education Authorities. Shanghai Is a Mixed City of Chinese and Foreigners and Is the Most Unharmonious Area in Our Country Today. Although Zhabei Tan Town and Pudong Near the Countryside Have Been Affected by the Erosion of Large Cities, People's Lives Still Retain the Relics of the Seventeenth and Eighteenth Centuries. The Nanjing Road Area Is All Modern in Scale. In This Complex and Unharmonious Environment, It Is Inevitable That People Will Wander and Have Nowhere to Go. Therefore, It Is Impossible to Delay Guiding the People's Knowledge in Life. All These Problems Are Closely Related to National Independence, Universal Civil Rights, and the Development of People's Livelihood. Colleagues Are Eager to Work Together With All People in Shanghai. We Also Hope That Famous People in Shanghai Will Provide Support and Guidance to Promote Education in Shanghai. Fortunately, National Education Is Fortunately. This Is a Declaration.

Fourth Elementary School Teacher Examination 11

County Education Bureau Orders All School Teachers to Comply

The Shanghai Education Bureau issued an order yesterday to all elementary school principals, stating: "Regarding the JiangSu Province Education Department's Order No. 5, it is stated that the experimental examination and verification of elementary school teachers is a crucial policy for alleviating the current shortage of teachers and also a method for carefully selecting talent and improving education. The Department has held several sessions and explained everything thoroughly, which should be understood by all. However, it has been found that many elementary school teachers in various counties still fill positions with unqualified teachers, and many personnel who should take the experimental examination and verification are avoiding the examination under various pretexts, which is contrary to the Department's intention of carefully selecting teachers. It is now decided that the fourth elementary school teacher experimental examination and verification will be held from April 3rd to 5th of the 22nd year [of the Republic, i.e. 1933]. The registration deadline is set from the date of receiving this Department's order until January 31st of the 22nd year. The registration fee is originally one yuan, but this session will be reduced to fifty cents to show consideration for the financial difficulties of elementary school teachers. All sub-district procedures and registration review procedures will be handled in accordance with the previous verification regulations. Once the registration and examination dates for this session are set, they will not be postponed. All Bureau Chiefs should follow the prescribed deadlines to notify all unqualified elementary school teachers to register and take the examination without allowing them to avoid it. After this session of verification, all unqualified elementary school teachers will not be allowed to be employed unless they have passed the verification examination. The Department is determined to rectify the teaching profession and will not show any leniency. Elementary school teachers who should take the experimental examination and verification should not hesitate and mislead themselves. In addition to separate orders, this order is issued to instruct the Bureau Chief to comply and publicize it widely. This is of utmost importance." Upon receiving this order, in addition to separate orders, this order is issued to instruct the school principal to inform all teachers who should take the experimental examination and verification to register before the deadline and not to delay and mislead themselves. This is of utmost importance.

Shanghai University Promotes Rural Improvement 12

The faculty and students of Shanghai University have always been enthusiastic about rural education and have worked hard to promote rural work in recent years. They have established rural service centers near the university, such as free elementary schools, public baths, and clinics, which have achieved considerable results. Students have also organized self-improvement groups that often go to the countryside during their spare time to get close to rural farmers, using methods such as talks and lectures to promote national awareness, instill general knowledge, and guide reading and learning, striving for all grassroots national salvation work, so that the countryside and schools can be assimilated to popularize education and improve the knowledge level of the masses. It is reported that a large-scale rural carnival will be held on campus on November 12th, the birthday of the late Dr. Sun Yat-sen, to exhibit domestic goods and perform educational entertainment to arouse the interest of rural farmers in school education. Preparations are currently underway.

China Vocational School, located on Yingxun Road, Lujiabang, West Gate, has been founded for several years. Charity Basketball Game Postponed 19

A Provisional Meeting Was Held Yesterday

The charity basketball game to aid the Northeast, initiated by the Overseas Chinese Middle School, was originally scheduled to begin this week. However, due to the unfinished repairs of the China Basketball Hall, it must be postponed until November 2nd before it can begin. The organizing committee held a provisional meeting yesterday to discuss the matter at length. The resolution is as follows: 1. All teams that have registered must send a deposit of ten yuan to the Sports Department of the Overseas Chinese Middle School, Xining Road, Charity Game Office before 6:00 PM on October 28th (Friday). Late submissions will be considered as non-participation (the deposit will be returned after the game is over. If a team is absent or late for a game, the deposit will be confiscated and used for charity, and their qualification for the game will be revoked). 2. The game time is set from 6:00 PM to 9:00 PM, and the distribution is as follows: 6:00-7:00 PM Middle School Group, 7:00-8:00 PM Women's Group, 8:00-9:00 PM University Group. 3. The game order will be determined after the number of confirmed teams has been collected. 4. All games will adopt an elimination system. 5. The number of people per team shall not exceed ten for men and twelve for women, including managers and coaches. In addition, all must purchase tickets to enter. 6. The game rules will adopt the basketball rules of 1931-1932 printed by the Sports Association. The new rules of 1932-1933 will not be applied for the time being. 7. The office is located in the Sports Department of the Overseas Chinese Middle School, Seymour Road. If you have any questions, please contact the office directly.

World Diving Championship 20

Smith's Performance Last Night Was a Great Success

Smith and Samanger, the world diving champions, gave their third performance at the Westerners Youth Association Swimming Pool at 9:00 PM last night. All 300 seats were filled. The performance was divided into three acts. The first act was platform diving, with the two taking turns performing a variety of tricks, which won the audience's applause. The second act was a slapstick comedy about learning to dive, which incorporated scientific methods into humor. In addition to laughing heartily, the audience also learned the essentials of learning to dive. The last act was Smith's solo performance of various swimming postures, which was helpful for beginners. The performance ended at around 10:00 PM.

New Basketball Techniques (10) (9) (Not Allowed) (Reprint)

Written by Clailo Burcky

Translated by Zhang Guodong and Qian Yiqin

Charles T. Black's Nicholas University basketball team was famous in last year's Six Giants League. Black has a tactic of using left-handed hook passes and clever feints and sudden movements. In this tactic, No. 1 receives the pass from No. 4 in the penalty area. No. 2 leads the defender to the arc of the penalty area to block No. 5's defense. No. 5 can take this opportunity to rush to the basket. He (No. 5) receives the left-handed hook pass from No. 1 at that spot and gently lifts it into the basket from the basket.

Song Ziwen Attends the Executive Yuan Meeting 21

Flewing to the Capital This Morning

Song and Wu Visited Chairman Lin Yesterday to Report

Acting President of the Executive Yuan Song Ziwen, regarding the Shandong Provincial Government Chairman Han Fuqu's telegram requesting resignation, the Executive Yuan will hold a meeting today (Tuesday) to discuss retaining him. Song has been approved to fly to the capital this morning. Zhang Shouyong, senior consultant of the Ministry of Finance, may accompany him. Before leaving, Song, accompanied by Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng, went to Father Jin Road at 11:30 AM yesterday to visit National Government Chairman Lin Sen to report on all recent central government matters. Song and others talked for half an hour. At around 12:00 PM, Song and Wu left first. According to Song's words to various news agencies, the visit to Chairman Lin was only to report, and Lin is expected to go to the capital in a day or two. The central government has not made any decisions on whether to reorganize the Fujian Provincial Government. Regarding the resignation of the Shandong Provincial Government Chairman Han Fuqu, the central government should retain him. Now, in addition to personally sending a telegram in my personal capacity to advise him not to have any thoughts of resigning, the Executive Yuan will hold a meeting tomorrow (i.e. today) to discuss the matter. I am approved to fly to the capital tomorrow morning (i.e. this morning) to participate in the discussion.

Overseas Chinese Association 22

Farewell to Weng Zhaoyuan

Welcome Zhang Yongfu and Du Huisheng

The Shanghai Overseas Chinese Association hosted a banquet at the East Asia Restaurant on Nanjing Road at 7:00 PM last night to welcome Singaporean leader Zhang Yongfu and Honolulu Chamber of Commerce President Du Huisheng, and to bid farewell to General Weng Zhaoyuan who is going abroad. Attendees included Xu Qian, Zhang Zhiben, Xue Dubi, Xiao Jishan, Fu Rulin, Chen Wulie, Zhang Yongfu, Du Huisheng, Weng Zhaoyuan, Ma Kui, Guo Shun, Zhao Yu, Li Denghui, Wang Hanqiang, Xiang Kangyuan, Chen Weixin, Wu Mai, Yan Bowei, Huang Jianzhong, Wu Shan, Pan Gongzhan, and more than sixty others. Chairman Xu Jigong presided over the meeting and recorder Yao Zhenlong. First, the chairman gave a speech, saying that today the association welcomes Mr. Zhang and President Du and bids farewell to General Weng. He is deeply grateful for the presence of all of you. Mr. Zhang is an old friend of Dr. Sun Yat-sen. He and Dr. Sun organized the Tongmenghui to create the Republic of China. General Weng's Songhu battle achievements were for the nation to fight for survival and for the country to fight for glory. He also mentioned the fact that President Du loves the motherland.
