Wang Maoqing 28

Invents Anti-Aircraft Flying Arrow

Please Request Funds from the Northeast Volunteer Army Support Team to Urgently Manufacture

The Association Does Not Know the Truth and Has Sent a Letter to Han Fuqu to Inquire

In recent months, Chinese people have invented many explosive munitions, such as flying mines and flying arrows, which are mostly used to shoot down airplanes for anti-aircraft purposes. However, due to the fact that the inventors and manufacturers are limited by funds, they often use surgery. Sometimes the results are very good, and sometimes they fail during the experiment. Recently, Wang Maoqing from Hebei, who has a long military history, has invented a flying arrow that can shoot 4,000 meters horizontally and 3,000 meters vertically. It is more than enough to shoot down airplanes with it. He has tested it in Jinan, and Han Fuqu is very appreciative. Because of the limited capital, he has been unable to manufacture it on a large scale. Yesterday, he sent a special letter to the Northeast Volunteer Army Support Team in Shanghai, requesting funds to be urgently manufactured for the warriors outside the Guan to resist the enemy. The letter is as follows: Respected directors, I am pleased to learn that your association's representatives have repeatedly developed national salvation undertakings and have promoted many more things. I am deeply impressed. However, the situation is evolving, and people have not fully realized their talents. Politics remains the same, and the country has not escaped its difficulties, so that grand plans and great strategies have not been developed. We are all sad. Recently, Wang Maoqing from Hebei Province, who has a long military career and leads artillery troops, and several members of his department (who have all retired) have used the intelligence of the descendants of Yan and Huang to invent an anti-aircraft weapon with great effectiveness, the flying arrow. The raw materials are purely domestic. It can shoot 4,400 meters horizontally and 3,000 meters vertically. The bombing power is around 30 meters to 40 meters. The shape of the gun barrel is similar to an anti-aircraft gun. Each cost is only 25 yuan. Each flying arrow costs 5 yuan (excluding wages). Anti-aircraft is better than anti-aircraft guns, and defending against the enemy is better than mortars and plane-shooting guns. The value is small, the manufacturing is easy, and the effectiveness is great. It is truly the most profitable defensive weapon in the current national crisis. It has been tested several times in Jinan, and everyone exclaimed in wonder. Han Fuqu, the chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, was very pleased to see the results and decided to build 30 gun barrels and 300 flying arrows. However, the colleagues thought that the people in the Northeast were suffering from the Japanese invaders every day, and the volunteer army lacked anti-aircraft weapons. If they could manufacture some and try to transport them there, the cost would not be much, but the benefit would be great. The current difficulty is that they lack capital to purchase ordinary tools such as machine beds and presses. The current manufacturers are purely handmade, and the production is small and time-consuming. On average, it takes three days of work to manufacture a flying arrow (eight hours a day, for a total of 24 hours). If there is machine manufacturing, it will take less time and produce more. It is planned to ask your association to promote and bring the gun barrels and flying arrows from here to Shanghai for testing. If you are satisfied, you will raise tens of thousands of yuan in capital to choose a site to set up a civilian anti-aircraft flying arrow factory and engage in urgent production specifically for foreign countries. The country is fortunate, and the nation is fortunate. Is it possible to ask for instructions? Liu Yimin, Wang Maoqing, Northeast Volunteer Army Support Team, thanks. The Northeast Volunteer Army Support Team is still unaware of the truth of this matter, so it will first send a letter to Han Fuqu, the chairman of Shandong Province, today to inquire whether it is true, and then try to find a way.

Three Watch Shops Were Bombed Yesterday 29

Sun Guangxing Watch Shop, Qipan Street, Sun Guangxing Watch Shop was jointly established by Ningbo merchants. Its manager is Cao Xiaoquan. A month ago, the shop received warning letters from the Anti-Traitor Corps and other groups and published a statement in the newspaper. At around 4:15 PM yesterday, a young man suddenly delivered a warning letter from the Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Corps to the shop's counter. All the partners opened it and looked at it. Before they could read a few lines, a bomb suddenly landed outside the door in front of the glass watch cabinet in the shop. It exploded instantly, and iron fragments flew around. All the partners hurriedly dodged. The glass windows displaying watches facing the street on the left and the glass windows of the long glass cabinet on the left in the shop were all destroyed by the explosion. There were also five or six holes in the ceiling. At the same time, a flower seller passing by outside the door was also scratched on his left flank by iron fragments, but it was very light. After the police received the report, they immediately sent detectives to investigate and collected the broken iron fragments and letters and took them to the police station for filing.

Samsung Watch Shop, Fuzhou Road, Samsung Public Concession, also suddenly received a warning letter from the Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Corps at around yesterday afternoon. Before long, a bomb flew in from outside the door and hit the wall in the shop's accounting room without exploding. The people in the shop were all pale with fright and immediately reported to the police, who sent detectives to investigate. All the unexploded bombs and warning letters were taken away by the police for filing.

Yuchang Watch Shop, Fuzhou Road, Yuchang Watch Shop also received a warning letter from the Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Corps and was thrown a bomb at the same time, which landed near the glass cabinet in the shop. The cabinet was destroyed in the explosion, but no one was injured. Afterwards, the shop denied the incident to the investigators.

Seeking Effective Sanctions

It Is Necessary to Strengthen One's Own Power First

Since the occurrence of the Lu War followed by the Sichuan War, the General Association of the Anti-Civil War Grand Alliance has repeatedly telegraphed to dissuade and dispatched representatives to petition for a cessation of hostilities. However, all efforts have failed to achieve practical results. Therefore, the association deeply feels that in order to seek truly effective methods to stop civil wars, it must first strengthen its own power. It plans to establish branches in major provinces and cities and broadly recruit members, so that when incidents occur, there will be popular support to carry out sanctions. The association's recent progress in establishing branches is recorded as follows:

Telegram from Tianjin Branch: The Tianjin branch has now been formally established. After its establishment, the branch sent a telegram to the General Association, stating that foreign aggression is increasingly urgent and the League of Nations is about to discuss the Far East issue. At this critical juncture, how can we bear further civil wars? The Tianjin branch has now been established, and all sectors are enthusiastically supporting it. The press is also willing to unite the national press to collectively advocate. If the people can awaken to the ambitions of the warlords, they can ultimately be restrained. The situation is critical. We hope that the General Association will quickly telegraph the whole country to urge the establishment of branches to facilitate progress. Sincerely, Tianjin Branch.

Actively Preparing for the Establishment of Branches: At the second standing committee meeting of the association, it was resolved to first organize branches in six locations: Beiping, Tianjin, Hankou, Nanjing, Guangzhou, and Chongqing. In addition, in Qingdao and Jinan, Zhang Boling, a standing committee member, once gathered representatives of local organizations to discuss the methods. In Changsha, the preparatory work is being handled by standing committee members Hu Shuhua and Fu Yueqi.

Representatives Depart for Jingzhen: At the seventh daily standing committee meeting of the association, it was decided to publicly recommend Standing Committee Member Liu Zhanen to go to Zhenjiang and Nanjing to contact and urge the business and academic communities in those areas to prepare for the establishment of branches, and to hold lectures or discussions. Mr. Liu is scheduled to depart for Zhenjiang by the early train this morning (25th), leave Zhenjiang for Beijing on the afternoon of the 26th, and return to Shanghai from Beijing on the afternoon of the 27th. The association has sent letters in advance to Standing Committee members Yu Xiaochuan and Lu Xiaobo in Zhenjiang, and Pu Yangshan and Wu Yifang in Nanjing, to arrange for the leaders of local legal organizations to gather and discuss everything at the time.

Especially today, after the January 28th Incident, the decline of the national economy is even more severe. Today, our conference has held its closing ceremony. After the closing ceremony, I hope that all sectors will pay attention to the manufacturing products after this exhibition. If there are any shortcomings, how should we seek improvements using scientific methods? What kind of goods are needed by the people, but China is still lacking? We should find ways to manufacture and make up for these deficiencies. Furthermore, to make the people of the whole country interested in using national goods, we must start with excellent products and reduce prices. At the same time, the people and the government should cooperate to protect industry and commerce. However, the development of industry and commerce depends on both the development of production and the promotion of sales. If there is developed production without a large sales market, the danger is even greater. However, China is vast, with a large population. However, although we cannot compete with the world's advanced industrial countries in reality, we must always strive to develop and compete with the great powers in spirit after this meeting. I hope that the national industrial and commercial sectors and the people will pay attention together, so as not to let down the great significance of holding this meeting."

It should be known that the significance of the National Goods Exhibition is to display national goods from all over the country in one room for everyone to refer to, so that the people know to use national goods, and at the same time, national goods manufacturers can compare each other. The better ones should strive for perfection, and the inferior ones should strive for improvement. The opening ceremony is certainly important, but the closing ceremony is even more important. The so-called closing is only a closing in form. Its significance in promoting and encouraging is not a permanent closing. Therefore, I hope that after the closing, manufacturers should deeply remember the impressions of the exhibition and keep them in their minds. I hope that the exhibition next year will be even better. The people should not only criticize the quality of national goods but also take action and not just talk."

City Chamber of Commerce Sends Letter to Woolen Mill Industry 34

Encouraging the Imitation of Serge and Woolen Fabrics

Starting with Those That Are Easier to Imitate

Yesterday, the City Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Shanghai Woolen Mill Industry Association, stating: "Respectfully, we received a letter from the Footwear Industry Association stating that on October 8th, your Chamber sent a letter stating, 'Now, the National Goods Promotion Committee of our Chamber, Director Fang Jiaobo, has sent a letter with the minutes of the third meeting, in which the second item states, "We are sending a letter to the industry associations of each industry to find out the names and uses of national products in their industry that can replace foreign goods and reply within this month for promotion purposes," which was submitted to the 14th Standing Committee meeting and resolved to handle it accordingly. Therefore, we hereby submit this matter, as we are not specialized in manufacturing and have no products that can replace foreign goods. The Executive Committee claimed after discussing under the Fourth Executive Committee Meeting that before the anti-Japanese boycott movement in Shanghai, the industry had been using a type of lake green leather, lead wire nails, hemp thread, and other items. These were all Japanese goods. Now, they are all replaced by domestic goods. Hatred of goods must have disappeared. It has been found that the shoe upper serge, tribute, and felt, black velvet used for winter warm shoes all come from Europe and the West, and their sales are the widest, which is very concerning. If we consider our country's current situation, the footwear material used in the prosperous area of Shanghai during the late Qing Dynasty was Nanjing-produced satin damask, but it was fragile and easy to tear, and it was easy to fluff and get dirty. By the early years of the Republic of China, Europe and the West released a new type of woolen material tribute serge and winter shoes using felt and black velvet. It has a soft texture and no fragility or fluffing defect. We experimented with making shoe materials and were quite welcome by customers, so the market for tribute suddenly been taken over by wool from imported goods. The reason for this is that our country is sticking to old ways and industry does not know how to improve. The pain in the heart is even shoes for life are essential, with the largest number of sales. It is necessary to address is the leak, it will be difficult to make up for the situation. Extravagant talks about invigorating industry and promoting national goods are empty words and cannot make up for it. We should ask your Association to pay attention to raising funds to organize woolen mills and improve their products so that they can stop the leakage. So, to promote national goods will not be just empty words, this is a very important matter." The woolen mill industry in this city has several of them. Rather than re-raising funds to start a business, as the Association said, it seems better to ask the existing factories to study imitation or improve them, which is more cost-effective and labor-saving. After all, can the factories in this city find ways to imitate or make improvements on all kinds of wool? The factories of your Association should be invited to carefully discuss with the factories. If they are limited by technology or capital, they may work together to start with those that are easier to imitate in order to save the leakage. Hopefully, the promotion of national goods will not be an empty slogan.

He completed his work yesterday and went north last night, first to Vladivostok, and then took the Siberian Railway train to Zaisan, Central Asia, to return to his original consular post.

Your Director-General cannot and does not want to deny this observation. Ministry of Railways Instructs All Railways 42

Transferring Old Uniforms to Disaster Victims

Adding a Mark to Avoid Parading

Regarding the situation of disaster relief in disaster areas such as Northeast and Henan provinces, Mr. Zhu Ziqiao telegraphed the Ministry of Railways to instruct all railway bureaus to raise donations. In addition to ordering all railway bureaus to raise donations within their capabilities, the Ministry of Railways also considered that the disaster situation in various provinces is serious and in urgent need of relief. It is feared that the donations raised will not be enough to meet the needs, and the old uniforms stored by the railways over the years must be quite a few. It is a pity to abandon them. It is better to transfer them for relief. However, after they are distributed, it is difficult to guarantee that there will be no bad people who wear them and take the opportunity to parade. We must be cautious from the beginning and stipulate that a large mark be added to this item of old uniforms to identify them. The Ministry of Railways specially telegraphed all railway bureaus the day before yesterday to quickly list all old uniforms, whether they are single, double, woolen, cotton, coats, trousers, and report them to the Ministry for overall planning, designating distribution locations and adding marking styles, so that they can be transported separately to various provinces for distribution to provide winter relief and the gospel of the people in the disaster area.

Jisheng Society's Jiangxi Relief Report 47

The Shanghai Chinese Jisheng Society recently received a letter from Director Li Yunmen in Nanchang, stating that the stone embankment section of Futouwei Tiexian Lake was completed on the 2nd of this month, and 70% of the dam soil has been excavated. The project is substantial, and there are no floating expenses. The local people, especially the farmers, are very grateful, which is gratifying. On the 5th, he inspected the Niuwei Sluice Gate at Dayouwei, and on the 8th, he returned to the province to arrange everything at Yinjiatang in Futouwei, which has also started excavation of the foundations. Eighty percent of the gravel required for these two sections has been purchased and transported, and timber is currently being transported for piling. With sunny weather, work is being accelerated, and it is estimated that the entire project can be completed within two months. The benefits to farmland from the completion of this section will be even greater. The previously brought relief funds have been withdrawn from the Nanchang branch of the Bank of China for 2,000 yuan. The late rice here has recently been harvested and is more abundant than in previous years. However, the rice price is too low, with each stone of rice priced at about 2 yuan, which inevitably causes farmers to suffer in secret. Knowing that the attention is not relaxed, I respectfully submit this report. China is founded on agriculture, and it is necessary to diligently repair water conservancy and build embankments and ponds to reduce disasters and increase production to save the bankrupt rural economy. It is hoped that enthusiastic people from all walks of life will rise up to assist in the completion of the projects to be repaired everywhere.

The shipping industry in Shanghai received news from Yingkou that the Yu Da Company, a shipping company run by Chinese in Yingkou, has three ships that operate from the Northeast to Shanghai and various ports in Beiyang. Regarding business operations, they are still allowed to operate, but in terms of sovereignty, they are taking an interventionist approach. However, they are strictly keeping it secret from the outside world, and even the Shanghai branch is not being informed of the inside story. This is just the first step of their actions. Since this incident occurred, the national shipping companies in Yingkou and Andong have been quite disheartened.

He especially praised several works in the first part, "Chinese Painting," such as "Ink Lion," "Great Pine," and "Eagle," for their majestic vitality that others could not match. In the second part, "Pre-European Travel Works," such as "Qianmen" and "Leifeng Pagoda," he praised the paintings' simple and solid colors and magnificent atmosphere. Page 11

Local News Two

Father's Obituary of a Lawsuit Monger

Numerous Important Figures Write Praises

Reprinted from Ye Huiduo's Obituary

Chiang, Lin, Wang, and Sun All Wrote Extensively

Chiang Ordered an Arrest After Receiving a Secret Report

The Person Is on the Run, a Large Number of Obituaries Seized

Yesterday morning, the First Special District Court heard a peculiar case. The facts were that a Zheng surname from Shaoxing forged an obituary, reprinted praises and inscriptions from important figures of the party and the state, and swindled money under false pretenses. He was secretly accused to Chiang, the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission in Hankou. Chairman Chiang secretly ordered Mayor Wu Tiecheng to thoroughly investigate the case. Mayor Wu ordered Director Wen of the Public Security Bureau to send personnel to the residence of the Zheng surname along with the police to seize a large number of forged exhibits. However, the Zheng surname had already fled upon hearing the news. Yesterday, the First Special Court held a hearing and decided to temporarily hand over the seized exhibits to the Public Security Bureau for safekeeping, pending the arrest of Zheng to verify the case. The details are recorded below.

Zheng Wenxiang, also known as Zheng Qifeng, a Shaoxing native, residing at No. 7 Qinghefang, Zhejiang Road, Public Concession, specializes in lawsuit mongering. He has a "Law Office for the Protection of Human Rights" set up in his residence. There are more than ten listed lawyers, all of whom are the best among Shanghai lawyers. The interior is decorated magnificently, resembling a wealthy businessman's villa. Throughout the day, it is filled with distinguished guests and visitors, resembling Mengchang's three thousand retainers.

Father's Obituary: At the beginning of this month, Zheng suddenly issued a large number of obituaries, roughly stating that "My late father, Duke Dehe, passed away at the residence in the countryside due to illness at the hour of Chou on the 19th day of the twelfth month of the lunar calendar in the 20th year of the Republic of China, at the age of 59. We have carefully selected the 8th day of the tenth month (November 5th) for burial in Shanbei and have chosen the 16th day of the tenth month (the 17th day of the ninth month in the lunar calendar) to receive condolences at the Fuxing Garden Restaurant on Pingwang Street, Wuma Road." The obituary was printed on a four-fold hardcover paper and was artistically designed.

Important Figures' Praises: The most noteworthy thing in the obituary is the portrait of Zheng's father in the center of the cover. At the top is "Portrait of Mr. Zheng Dehe" inscribed by Cai Yuanpei, and below the portrait are the four characters "Benevolent Heart and Heroic Spirit" inscribed by Chiang, the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, in seal script, with "Mr. Dehe Forever" signed above and "Chiang Kai-shek" signed below. The second page is personally inscribed by Chairman Lin of the National Government with "Merit Remains in the Republic," the third page is inscribed by Sun Ke with "Name Resounds in Shanghai," and the last page is inscribed by General Cai Tingkai with twelve sentences of praise. At the bottom is inscribed by Wang Zhaoming with "Heroic Demeanor Still Remains." Each person's name is followed by a vermilion seal.

Secret Accusation of Forgery: Unexpectedly, after Zheng's obituary was issued, someone saw through that the obituary was forged, intending to swindle money under false pretenses, and secretly accused Director Wen of the Public Security Bureau. Director Wen was initially hesitant and secretly ordered the Detective Team to thoroughly investigate. While the investigation was underway, the Municipal Government suddenly received a secret order from Chiang, the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission in Hankou, along with a copy of the obituary of the late Shanghai gentleman Ye Huijun and Zheng's obituary.

Replacing One With Another: Chairman Chiang's letter roughly stated that he had received a secret accusation that Zheng Wenxiang, a Shaoxing native residing at No. 7 Qinghefang, Zhejiang Road, Public Concession, had illegally used the inscriptions and seals of important figures of the party and the state, and issued obituaries indiscriminately, intending to swindle money under false pretenses. He also attached a copy of Zheng's forged obituary, requesting an arrest. After investigation, it was found that Zheng's obituary was indeed a forgery, completely reprinted from the obituary of the late Shanghai gentleman Ye Huijun. After comparison, except for "Portrait of Mr. Zheng Dehe" inscribed by Central Committee Member Cai Yuanpei, which was completely forged, and "Heroic Demeanor Still Remains" inscribed by President Wang, which was reprinted from the obituary of Secretary-General Chu Minyi, the rest was completely identical and reprinted.

Investigation Without Success: The letter concluded by ordering the Municipal Government to investigate and handle the matter properly. After receiving the order, Mayor Wu immediately handed it over to Director Wen, who ordered the Detective Team to send personnel to the residence of Zheng on Qinghefang, Zhejiang Road, along with the Chinese and foreign detectives in charge. However, Zheng had already fled upon hearing the news, and a large number of unfinished forged obituaries and a copy of Ye Huijun's real obituary were seized on the spot.

Verification After Capture: The seized evidence was immediately escorted to the police station and transferred to the First Special District Court. The case was heard yesterday morning in the Eighth Tribunal of the First Special District Court. Because Zheng had not been captured, the evidence was temporarily handed over to Qi Haitian, the leader of the Detective Team of the Public Security Bureau, for safekeeping, pending the arrest of the suspect Zheng for verification.

Wu Huaichun 54

Case of Defiling Sisters

The Younger Sister Died First, and the Elder Sister Was Abandoned

The Hearing Was Held Yesterday, With Both Sides Giving Their Accounts

The Case Was Postponed Because Shi Chen Was Not Present

The Judge Ordered Wu to Appear in Court Next Time

Wu Huaichun, who resides in Yinyu Company at No. 24 Jiwufang, Ximen Road, was recently accused by Shi Chen, a woman from Changshu, of raping her second daughter, Lingyu, causing her death, and of raping, abducting, and abandoning her eldest daughter, Jinghua. Lawyers Wu Peng and He Yijun filed a lawsuit against him in the Second Special District Court for the above crimes. Yesterday was the date for the hearing of this case. Judge Li Changnian summoned both parties to the First Tribunal for questioning. Since the plaintiff, Shi Chen, was ill and did not appear in court, Shi Jinghua first stated that she is 19 years old, from Changshu, and currently resides in the home of relatives in Dexingli, North Sichuan Road. Her sister initially came to Shanghai with relatives to learn opera. After that, her whereabouts were unknown. In April of this year, she received a letter from her sister saying that she was ill in Shanghai, so her mother first came to Shanghai, and then she came to Shanghai, to take care of her sister's illness. On April 16 of this year, her mother went to the countryside to get clothes. At that time, she took care of her sister day and night and had not closed her eyes for six or seven nights. On April 24, Wu Huaichun said that such hard work might cause her to get sick, so he asked her to go to sleep peacefully tonight, and he would accompany her.

Wu then committed indecency. At that time, she was only wearing a pair of underpants. When she woke up, she was being pressed down by him. She wanted to scream, but Wu said that if her sister heard it, she would definitely die of anger, so she endured in silence. Her sister was four years younger than her and was only 15 years old this year. She initially lived in Fan Guilins house. Her mother knew Fan, and the relationship between Fan and Wu started this year. Her sister actually died because of the rape. Wu initially tricked her into marrying him, but she refused. Wu said that if she did not agree, they would die together. On the 15th day of the seventh lunar month, Wu went to Kunshan to pay respects to her sister's grave and then came to Shanghai to live in the Wuling Apartment for a total of one month and one day. At that time, her mother did not come with her, and she lived alone at night. Wu came at six o'clock in the morning and went to sleep again and came to accompany her in the evening and did not leave until ten o'clock because his family limited him to returning home by ten o'clock every night. After that, Wu did not come. On August 14, the Wuling Apartment accountant informed her that the room had expired, so she had no choice but to return home. She did not borrow money from him. The expenses in the apartment were paid by him, and there are invoices to prove it. She heard that Wu went to play in the business every day after that, so he did not come. Therefore, she is requesting

to prosecute him for the crime of rape and abandonment and for the death of her sister due to rape. Then, according to Wu Huaichun's statement, he is 47 years old, from Suzhou, and is a rental accountant for Yinyu Company, residing at No. 24 Jiwufang, Ximen Road. He met her sister, named Yunzhen (i.e., Lingyu), last year. She lived at No. 2 Zengrongli, Aige Road, doing business. Since No. 2 was Han Zhuang, he did not go there for a long time after he met Yunzhen in July last year.

This year, he went to play again and saw that Yunzhen was ill. Her illness was a cough. He then advised her family to seek medical treatment and rest quietly. At that time, Shi Chen was also in Shanghai. Around the 20th of March, Shi Chen said that it was not suitable to live here and begged him to find a place to recuperate, so he helped her move to the nearby Shiyinli. At that time, Fan Guilin said that Yunzhen was 18 years old, but Shi herself said that she was 15 years old. During her illness, he helped her seek medical treatment and often went there during the day. Later, Yunzhen's illness became more serious. Because Yunzhen had pledged 300 yuan to Fan, Fan saw that her illness was getting worse and came to ask for the money. Shi Chen then discussed it with him, and he lent her 300 yuan as a

future concubine. He also vaguely agreed. Later, she went to the Red Cross Hospital and died soon after. He had no physical relationship with Jinghua. Because he did not go to her house at night, she came to see her sister, which was the case. Besides, Yunzhen and her mother were both present. Wuling Apartment was rented for Jinghua to come to Shanghai to worship Yunzhen in the seventh lunar month at her request. At first, she said that she would stay for a few days, then she stayed for one month and one day, and he could not interfere. The expenses in Wuling Apartment were given to her for 50 yuan, and she lived alone. He did not live with her. He did not know Jinghua before because she came on May 9 to

see her sister's illness before they met. She once asked him

for a thousand yuan but he did not agree and asked him to recommend business for her fiancé, which he also did not agree to. He was afraid that she would hold a grudge because of this. Then, Judge Li ordered that the case was complicated, and Shi Chen was not present today, so the hearing was postponed, and he strictly ordered the defendant Wu Huaichun to appear in court next time, and then adjourned the court.

[P Special Police's Home Robbed>

Two Chinese Police Officers Rushed to the Scene Upon Hearing the Whistle

One Police Officer Was Injured, and the Thieves Fled in All Directions

Cai Liufu, a special police officer at the Xinzha Police Station in the Public Concession of Shanghai, lived at No. 281 Binlang Road. Yesterday at 6:20 PM, when Cai happened to be out, four robbers suddenly came to his house, each holding a handgun. Two thieves guarded the gate, and two thieves went inside, first confining his family members in a room and threatening them not to make a sound, and then began to search. Unexpectedly, one of his family members was not confined and secretly ran upstairs to take refuge in the east wing. They pushed open the window facing the street, frantically blew the whistle, and shouted "Catch the robbers!" Upon hearing the sound, the robbers panicked and quickly abandoned their belongings and fled through the gate. At this time, two patrolling Chinese police officers, No. 1478 and No. 14, happened to be passing by Putuo Road and heard the whistle and rushed to the scene. When the robbers saw them, they quickly pulled out their guns and fired four shots at them. Chinese police officer No. 14 could not dodge in time and was shot in the right waist. At the same time, a Chen surname man and a woman passing by the roadside were also injured by stray bullets in their hands. The robbers then fled in all directions. Chinese police officer No. 1478 chased after them but failed to catch them and returned to the original location to send Chinese police officer No. 14 to the police station to report everything and sent the injured men and women to Baolong and Guangren Hospitals for treatment. The injured Chinese police officer was transferred from the Putuo Road Police Station to the Police Hospital for treatment, and detectives were dispatched to pursue the robbers and investigate the case.

Accountants Association General Meeting 58

The Shanghai Accountants Association convened its autumn regular members' meeting yesterday at No. 4 Hong Kong Road. Eighty-nine members attended, and the meeting proceeded as scheduled. The presidium consisted of Yu Xiji, Wang Haifan, and Zhao Zuwei. Zhao Zuwei (3) reported on the purpose of the meeting and the progress made in the past six months. Wang Haifan reported on the income and expenditure status of the current session. (5) Jiang Wanping reported on the supervision of the association's affairs. (6) Chairman Yu Xiji discussed the proposals. (1) It was proposed that the sixth executive committee approved a letter from the Zhejiang Provincial Accountants Association, requesting that the regular fees for accountants joining both associations in the two regions be considered for modification. Because this matter involves amending the articles of association, it was proposed to submit it for discussion. It was resolved that it be incorporated into the discussion of amending the articles of association. (2) It was proposed that the seventh executive committee suggested that the association's articles of association, Chapter 3, Article 6, does not include an introducer, which is inconsistent with the application form. It was resolved that it be handled in conjunction with the amendment of the articles of association. (3) It was proposed that the eighth executive committee approved the third legal research committee's proposal to amend the Accountants Law and the association's articles of association. It was resolved that Articles 11 and 12 of the law not be deleted, Article 16 be submitted to the Ministry of Industry for interpretation, and Article 5 of the articles of association, originally "those who wish to practice in Shanghai and its surrounding areas," be changed to "those who wish to establish an office and practice in Shanghai." Furthermore, Articles 6 and 8 under the same article should be amended according to the comments, and Articles 10 and 11 should not be amended. (4) It was proposed that the eighth executive committee approved the third legal research committee's proposal that resolutions of the members' meeting should have the same effect as the association's articles of association. It was resolved that it be handed over to the executive committee for handling. (5) It was proposed that the fourth joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees approved the standing committee's proposal that there are six members who have been in arrears with regular fees for more than one year, and have been repeatedly sent letters and dispatched personnel to collect them, but have not yet paid. According to the articles of association, "members who fail to pay the association's regular fees for six months may be submitted by the executive committee to the members' meeting for expulsion." It was resolved that they be expelled in accordance with the articles of association and reported separately. (6) It was proposed that the fourth joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees approved the standing committee's proposal that there are fifteen old members who are still in arrears with the building fund. The spring members' meeting this year resolved that all payments should be made within two months. On June 24 of this year, the proposal was extracted and repeatedly sent letters and dispatched personnel to collect them, but payment has not yet been made. It was proposed for review and resolution that a deadline be set for collection. (7) It was proposed that the fourteenth joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees approved the standing committee's proposal that there are forty members who are in arrears with regular fees for more than six months, and have been repeatedly sent letters and dispatched personnel to collect them, but payment has not yet been made. It was proposed for review and resolution that a deadline be set for collection. (8) Chairman Wang Haifan discussed the proposal that Jiang Wanping and thirteen others proposed whether liquidators should bear the defendant's responsibility for debt relationships in entrusted cases. It was resolved to request the Ministry of Justice to issue an order for correction. (9) Members Wang Haifan and seven others proposed petitioning the government to establish a commercial court in this city. It was resolved that it be handed over to the executive committee for handling. (10) Members Sun Huan and five others proposed setting up reading rooms and lounges for accountants in courts at all levels nationwide. It was resolved that it be handed over to the executive committee for handling. (11) Xi Yushu and fourteen others proposed that the competent ministry be requested to jointly issue a new order with the Ministry of Justice to various judicial administrative agencies to issue detailed rules for accountants' services. It was resolved that it be handed over to the executive committee for handling. (12) Jiang Wanping and four others proposed finding a judge to entrust accountants with the duties of executors of wills. It was resolved that it be handed over to the legal affairs committee for handling, and that courts be requested to appoint accountants as executors of wills and bankruptcy administrators. (13) Lin Benzhong proposed that the association's journal should add a column on industrial and commercial laws and regulations to benefit members. It was decided that the executive committee should handle it. (14) Mu Zuyi proposed that the industry's job titles should be reported to the association at any time in order to statistically clarify the progress of business. It was resolved to postpone the discussion. (15) Chen Qixiang proposed, and Yuan Shude and Yao Yizhi seconded: (A) That the association publish an accounting weekly; (B) That the association stipulate the format of the documents that should be issued as stipulated in the detailed rules for accounting services and sell them accordingly to facilitate members; (C) That the National Government be petitioned to order the Legislative Yuan to amend Article 158 of the Company Law; (D) That the Legislative Yuan should be requested to clearly indicate when amending the Civil and Criminal Procedure Law regarding appraisers. It was resolved that (A) the association solicit whether members are willing to subscribe; (B) the legal affairs committee formulate the format, and the original proposer participate in the handling; (C) postpone the discussion; (D) the legal affairs committee propose a careful review of relevant accounting laws and regulations. (16) Temporary motions: (A) Xi Yushu proposed that the former Ministry of Industry and Commerce ordered that the annual final accounts of various companies should be certified by accountants. It was found that various companies often failed to comply. It was resolved to request the Ministry of Industry to reiterate the previous order and inform the administrative agencies of various provinces and cities to pay attention. (B) Li Fazhen proposed that in the future, all proposals of research value should be notified to all members in writing several days before the meeting to facilitate joint discussion. It was resolved that the executive committee should handle it accordingly. (C) Jiang Wanping proposed that it is quite difficult to convene meetings of various special committees. What are the remedies? It was resolved to send letters to all members requesting them to specify which special committee they are willing to assume duties on, and then submit them to the executive committee for separate reorganization. The meeting was adjourned after tea and refreshments.

Puyi Trust Company 59

Promoting Popular Trust Knowledge Movement

The trust business is an important economic system for developing assets and encouraging savings. It is almost well-known in European and American countries. However, the meaning of trust is not yet clear to the Chinese people, and there are many misunderstandings, which greatly hinder the development of individual and social economy. Puyi Trust Company, in view of this, took the lead in establishing a formal trust company in Shanghai and has been actively carrying out various trust businesses over the years. In order to expand its service scope, it has specially hired Mr. Hu Yigu, the former editor-in-chief and author of the Youth Association, to be responsible for promoting the popular trust knowledge movement and to compile trust industry books in both Chinese and English and other publications for research in all walks of life. It is determined to make trust knowledge popular throughout the society so that most people can get economic assistance. It is reported that the following six types are already being compiled: (1) Outline of Trust (2) Will and Property Management Law (3) Livelihood Trust (4) Life Insurance Trust (5) Commercial Insurance Trust (6) Custody and Agency Business. The meaning and value of various trusts are explained in detail in the above books, which are unprecedented reading materials in the society. The first type, "Outline of Trust," has now been published. Anyone who is interested in research can formally send a letter stating their name, address, and occupation to the company at No. 29 Nanjing Road for reading.

Shanghai County Government 60

Cracking Down on Coolies and Beggar Bosses Extorting Money

Shanghai County Government Announcement: Concerning the matter of an announcement, on the 15th of this month, the 30th district head meeting reported that the 5th district head, Xing Zhigang, proposed that the coolie associations in various townships, commonly known as industry associations, carry goods and arbitrarily charge high prices, relying on their numbers to coerce. Furthermore, during weddings and funerals in the countryside, they take the opportunity to divide up sections of land and hoard them. There are also beggar bosses who, regardless of weddings or construction, demand money. If they fail, they lead a group of beggars to the door to extort money, occupy the premises and refuse to leave, or seize food, causing all kinds of disturbances. The district learned that during the funeral of Yang Fusheng's son in Shangchun, the coolies from Chenxing Town went to Yang's house to freeload, gathered eight people, falsely claimed to be funeral palanquins, and volunteered themselves. The family provided them with food, and they all became drunk and disorderly, smashing dishes and plates in the kitchen because there was no food. Furthermore, when Sun Yunlong died in Qiaozhen, eight people from the funeral palanquin went to Sun's house and became drunk. The place was extremely small, but the coolies, regardless of the situation, occupied the hall and refused to leave. Such false extortion has long been severely prohibited in the Qing Dynasty, let alone under the flag of the Republic of China. In July of the tenth year of the Republic of China, the county government issued a notice to investigate and prohibit it. Now, after a long period of time, people are taking it lightly again. The winter season of weddings and funerals is approaching, and they may still repeat the old tricks and disturb the local area. Can we refer to the previous case and reiterate the strict prohibition, and publicly decide to implement it? After discussion, it was decided that the county government would issue an announcement and distribute it to various districts for prohibition. It is recorded that coolies and beggar bosses falsely extorting money and causing disturbances are indeed disrupting public safety and should be strictly prohibited to ensure peace. In addition to issuing orders to various district offices and public security bureaus to comply with the investigation and prohibition, this announcement is made to inform everyone. If any coolies or beggar bosses are found to be extorting money or causing disturbances from shops or residents, they will be immediately arrested and punished without leniency. Everyone must abide by this and not violate it. This announcement is hereby made.

During the January 28th Songhu Battle, the Jiangwan Epidemic Hospital opened the Red Cross Society's 15th Injured Soldiers Hospital and organized 13 rescue teams, treating a total of more than 500 people. After the war subsided, the Jiangwan Chongshan Hall organized a burial team to collect and bury more than 1,500 bodies of soldiers and civilians. They were enthusiastic about their work and sacrificed for the country. It is appropriate to commend them. Baoshan 62

Long-Distance Bus Driver Beaten

Since the Shanghai-Taicang Long-Distance Bus Company took over the Baoshan City Songjiang-Yangxing long-distance bus, the business has been smooth. However, the company's regulations stipulate that soldiers wearing uniforms only need to purchase half-price tickets, otherwise, if they do not have a free ticket, they must purchase tickets as usual. The day before yesterday morning, a soldier from Wusong to Baoshan was wearing a uniform but had no symbols and did not purchase a half-price ticket. He insisted on boarding the bus, and the ticket inspector politely dissuaded him. The soldier was resentful. Yesterday afternoon, at about 3:00 p.m., he gathered seven or eight companions and saw the bus driving from Yangxing to Baoshan being stopped by the soldiers near Sanguantang. The driver, Yu Chunquan, was dragged out of the bus and beaten with wooden sticks. Yu immediately fell to the ground, barely breathing. Later, he was sent to the hospital by someone. The assailants dispersed after their goal was achieved.

Inside the Changchun Tea Garden 63

Murderer of Detective Arrested

Multiple People Detained and a Handgun Confiscated

Hua Tanmu, Shang Wu, of the Huisi Detective Office, received a report on the 22nd of this month that there were many thieves inside the Changchun Tea Garden at No. 703 Tiantong Road. He led detectives Zhao Xiaohe, Huang Aqing, and Yin Ali to arrest them at about 10:00 a.m. However, one of the thieves was armed and opened fire upon seeing the detectives. The details have been previously reported in this newspaper. After the case occurred, all the detective offices paid attention to it. Hua Tanzhang, Su Changsheng, and Detective Zhou Guisheng of the Laozha Detective Office learned that the murderer in this case was Jiangbei native Yin Xinren, who was hiding at No. 46, Lane 603, Kangnaot Road, West Shanghai. They rushed to arrest Yin, along with accomplices Wang Bingnan, Zhou Fengshan, Zhao Yuzhen, Xu Mingcai, Ding Arong, Luo Xinmin, and others, all natives of Jiangbei, and a handgun and three bullets, and brought them back to the detective office. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the First Special Court's Criminal Division. The detective office's lawyer, Ru Baoyi, requested permission for detention because the case had not yet been investigated. Yin Xinren also confessed to opening fire to resist arrest. Judge Qian Hongye approved the detective office's request and ordered the defendants to be returned for further questioning. The corpse of Zhao Xiaohe was also inspected by the Special Court's Prosecutor Zhan Liangce, who confirmed that he had been shot and killed, and ordered his sister, Shen Zhao, to claim the body for coffin burial.

Pimping and Kidnapping of Wuxi Female Workers Sentenced 64

Li Xubai from Wuxi, Fang Zhongkun from Nanjing, Chen Ziying from Guangdong, and Zhu Zhang from Nanjing, recently lured Wuxi Lihua Weaving Factory female workers Wu Shouying and Wu Xiaomei to Shanghai and hid them in the Zhiyuan Hotel on Tianjin Road. Li and Fang forcibly raped them and planned to sell them to a brothel run by local woman Li Liu on Fuzhou Road. The case was uncovered and the men and women were arrested. The two women were temporarily sent to the Jiliang Institute pending review. This was previously reported. Yesterday morning, Judge Fu opened the court to continue the hearing. The detective office's lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, stated that the case was being rescheduled. Detectives searched the hotel where they were staying and found a letter from Zhu Zhang to Fang Zhongkun, stating that Fang had embezzled 40 yuan from a previous human trafficking case, so she was demanding it. From this, it can be seen that the defendants specialize in luring good women into prostitution and should be severely punished. He presented the seized letter as evidence. The defendant Li Xubai cunningly denied that the two women were sisters or close acquaintances, and said they did not work in Lihua and were actually private prostitutes. However, the two women denounced his words in court as pure fabrication. Fang Zhongkun claimed that Li only said that Wu Shouying was his wife and Xiaomei was a relative, and denied that the letter was written by him. Chen Ziying's testimony was also evasive. Zhu Zhang admitted to writing the letter to Fang to demand debt. Li Liu denied everything. As a result, Judge Fu sentenced Li and Fang to five years of imprisonment each, Chen Ziying and Zhu Zhang to three years of imprisonment each, and Li Liu to two months of imprisonment. Wu Shouying and Wu Xiaomei were sent to the Women and Children Relief Association. The letters were confiscated.

Lawsuit Following Marital Discord 69

Arguments Concluded, Awaiting Sentencing

Lu Xifan from Suzhou, the former manager of the National Hotel, and Wu Xiufeng, a woman from Guangdong, had a loving relationship for two years. Because she became pregnant, they entered into a marriage contract at the Ting En Law Firm in June this year. On the 25th of last month, Lu held a wedding at the Xindafang Hotel on Edward Road in the French Concession. Because the wedding was not completed, a marital dispute occurred. Wu Xiufeng went to Lu to argue, but was stopped and forced to marry. Because she refused, she was beaten. She filed a complaint with the French Detective Office against Lu and Zhou Qinglin, as well as lawyer Lu Ruizheng, for assault and battery. Lu Xifan also accused Wu's brother-in-law, Xia Yaoting, of gathering a crowd to assault him and cause injury. The Detective Office escorted Lu Xifan and Xia Yaoting to the Criminal Court of the Second Special Court to file a public prosecution. The details of the interrogation have been previously reported. The case has now been declared concluded, and the sentencing is scheduled. Wu Xiufeng, because the Detective Office did not file a public prosecution against Qinglin and Lu Ruizheng, hired lawyer Qin Zemin to file a criminal complaint with the Second Court, accusing Zhou and Lu of joint assault and demanding compensation for medical expenses. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 p.m., Judge Wu Fanglian of the Criminal Court 5 interrogated both parties, each accompanied by a lawyer. First, the plaintiff Wu Xiufeng stated that after she and Lu Xifan were engaged, she instructed him to notify her parents first and send gifts before arranging a wedding date. Unexpectedly, Lu did not inform her parents or send gifts, but suddenly went to her sister's house on September 25th to marry her at the Xindafang Hotel. Upon hearing the news, she and her sister went to the Xindafang Hotel to argue with Lu Xifan, but she was forced to marry him. She refused to leave and was stopped by Zhou Qinglin. Lu Xifan grabbed her hair and dragged her into the room, punching and kicking her. Lawyer Lu Ruizheng also forced her to marry Lu Xifan and kicked her, causing injury. Zhou Qinglin and Lu Ruizheng both denied the assault and said they were just trying to persuade her and were actually slandered, and verbally filed a counterclaim for damages for defamation. Lawyers for both sides argued for a long time about the name of the first defendant, Lu Xifan, listed on the plaintiff's complaint, since Lu had already been publicly prosecuted by the Detective Office and should not be sued again. The court then ordered the arguments to begin. As a result, the court declared the arguments concluded and scheduled the sentencing.

Yingchang Match Factory Fire Due to Carelessness 70

Losses Exceed 10,000 Gold

At about 6:05 a.m. yesterday morning, a worker at the Yingchang Match Factory No. 2 warehouse in Lujiadu, Pudong, suddenly noticed wisps of thick smoke coming from the bamboo weaving shed. The worker immediately sounded the alarm. It was during the shift change, and all the factory workers unlocked and pushed open the warehouse door, only to see a fierce fire inside that quickly broke through the roof. The factory's own water pool was opened, and eight or nine taps were used to vigorously extinguish the fire. However, the warehouse was full of already packaged matches, which were extremely flammable and difficult to extinguish for a while. The fire gradually subsided after burning for about an hour, but the pile of matches was so large that thick smoke was still coming out. The extinguishing work will continue throughout the night. In this incident, all six rooms of the No. 2 warehouse were completely destroyed. Three to four hundred boxes of Xiaoan matches and more than one hundred boxes of Beautiful Insurance and other brands were also burned. Most of the remaining matches were soaked in water and rendered useless. The total loss of houses and matches amounted to more than 10,000 gold. As for the cause of the fire, according to the factory director, Mr. Sun Muyi, the warehouse door has always been locked, and no one can enter. Therefore, there should be no cigarette butts falling in. It may be that mice chewed the paste on the paper wrapping and dragged out the matchsticks, and the match heads rubbed against the sandpaper, causing them to ignite. When the fire started, Director Zhang of District 3 and Director Yang of Precinct 1 supervised the police to maintain order at the scene. After the fire was extinguished, the factories resumed work as usual without any impact.

Shi Zhenghong Compiles Experimental Composition Method 71

Shi Zhenghong, a Chinese language teacher at Minzhi Primary and Secondary School in this city, has compiled a book entitled Experimental Composition Method based on his teaching experience. The materials are taken from the students' usual writing that has shortcomings, and the methods are organized clearly, the structure is precise, and everything is practical. It cannot be compared to the usual composition method books that are purely theoretical. It is now published and distributed by the Children's Bookstore on Zhejiang Road. Students from the third grade of elementary school to the third grade of junior high school can all read it, and it can also be used as a reference book for elementary school teachers. It is truly a good book on composition method.

[P] Qing'an Ship Captain Chen Yifan Departs Tomorrow [>] 73

Chen Yifan, the newly appointed captain of the Qing'an patrol ship of the Jiangzhe Fisheries Administration, has actively reorganized the ship's affairs since taking office. All officers and soldiers in the ship were deemed important talents, and were tested separately the day before yesterday to eliminate the old, weak and those who did not diligently perform their duties, so that public funds would not be wasted. Now that the winter defense is approaching, it is planned to depart tomorrow (the 26th) and go to the coastal areas to implement fishing protection.

Shengxin Lotus Society Lecture on Diamond Sutra Grand Event 74

The Shengxin Lotus Society is a place for lay Buddhists to study Buddhism, and it focuses on the Pure Land sect. The society was founded in Peiping more than ten years ago and has recently established a Shanghai branch at No. 712, Cihui Lane, Weihaiwei Road, Seymour Road. Now, Mr. Jiang Weinong, an old lay Buddhist in the society, has been earnestly requested by the society members for many years to lecture on the Diamond Sutra, and has been lecturing in the society every Tuesday and Friday evening from 7:30 p.m. to 9:00 p.m. He has lectured twice. It is said that this old man truly understands and is well-versed in this wonderful scripture. The audience is delighted, and he can also use skillful words to promote the supreme truth in Buddhism during the lectures.

Judge Feetham's Report on the Shanghai International Settlement, Volume IV (2) 84

B. The Position of Committees within the International Settlement

1. According to the existing situation, the main benefit that the Board of Directors derives from the use of the committee system is the benefit listed under heading III above, namely, the preliminary consideration of various important issues by the committees and the submission to the Board of Directors of the conclusions and recommendations on those issues contained in their minutes. The benefit under heading I is the result of the division of labor, and the extent to which this benefit is enjoyed is very limited because the committees have no executive power. The benefit described under heading II, which comes from the committees having the power to represent the final decision of the Board of Directors, cannot be said to have been enjoyed for the same reason. With regard to the benefit under heading III, which comes from the committees serving the Board of Directors in a purely advisory capacity, I believe that a more specific provision should be made as described above (Note 7) to ensure that the Board of Directors always has a committee report before submitting any important matter for resolution. This is the power of the Board of Directors.

2. One characteristic of the committee system developed in the International Settlement is that it includes members temporarily appointed by the Board of Directors. These members are not directors of the Board of Directors, but are either representatives of a particular section of society or have special knowledge or experience of the matters discussed by the committees. The inclusion of temporary members in the committee is an expedient strategy adopted to overcome some of the difficulties caused by the fact that the number of directors is subject to the restrictions of the Land Regulations. As a result, the Board of Directors can draw on outside talent and allow the majority of social leaders to participate in part of the work of the committee, so that the Board of Directors can more fully represent an entire society in the performance of its administrative duties.

3. However, the Land Regulations stipulate that "the Board of Directors may elect officers from among the directors to organize committees" (Article 23). Therefore, the method of joining committees as non-directors has not been authorized by the Land Regulations. Part of the legal defects in the committee organization law has been pointed out. "Therefore, each committee is only an advisory body and does not have the power to execute within the scope of recognition" (Note 8). The result of not granting executive power to the committees is that most committees are only convened when particularly important matters are deemed necessary to be brought to the attention of the committees, rather than holding meetings on a regular basis at short intervals.

4. In addition, there is another reason for the trend to reduce the number of committee meetings in the past, that is, when problems arise from time to time, the matter is discussed with the members by circulating documents instead of convening a committee. This method was very common in the past. The method used is to send a memorandum stating the issue to be decided, together with all the letters and reports related to the issue in the archives, to each member for circulation, and to ask each member to write down his opinion on the memorandum. If the result of the consultation is that the members agree, the issue is considered to have been decided. However, if the members disagree, the issue is reserved for consideration at a future committee meeting. The Board of Directors and the committees of the Public Works Department have limited use of this method, but at one time it was used frequently, so that the directors and members spent a lot of time paying attention to the circulated notes and the attached documents, which was very tiring. This is because the directors and members could not read the documents at their convenience, but had to put aside other matters that were being handled and immediately pay attention to the documents circulated by the Public Works Department, and then they could decide on their opinions and write them on the documents and immediately forward the documents to the second member, who also had to study the documents in the same way and write down his opinions.

5. Although the method of consulting by circulating documents is still in use to some extent, as far as I know, in part because of the disposition of matters by the Director-General, the number of documents circulated has been greatly reduced in recent times. The English name of the Director-General was formerly DirectorGeneral, but is now SecretaryGeneral. Some of the issues that used to be discussed with the Board of Directors or committees have now been authorized to the Director-General to have a wider scope to consider and handle.

6. The foreseeable result of depriving committees of any executive power is that a large amount of trivial work is left entirely to the directors themselves. However, as far as I can tell, this is not actually the case, except perhaps when the method of circulating documents is used extensively.

7. As far as I have observed, the agenda of the Board of Directors' regular meetings is not filled with a large number of trivial matters. If we consider the administrative scope of the Public Works Department, the number of special issues that are actually handled and decided by the Board of Directors at its weekly regular meetings is relatively small.

8. I believe that the reason why this is so is that, in fact, although the committees have no executive power, the main officials of the Public Works Department, generally speaking, the heads of the various departments, and specifically, the Director-General and the Director of Finance, are allowed to exercise and have exercised extensive executive power to carry out the actual work of administration. For most issues that are considered routine, they can be handled on their own authority without having to specifically submit the issues to the Board of Directors and committees for consideration.

9. The recently revised Board of Directors Rules and Regulations and the Regulations on the Duties of the Main Officials of the Public Works Department (Note 9) both reflect the situation described above. The duties of the committees are described as being only advisory, and even in terms of the advisory position of the committees, there is no provision specifying which issues should be submitted to the committees for consideration, except in very few cases, in order to protect the advisory position of the committees. The regulations explicitly grant executive power to the heads of the various departments for a limited number of issues. In addition, there are several provisions from which it can be inferred that this power can usually be used by the heads of the various departments in the course of ordinary administrative work. As for how the use is restricted, there is no clear provision. It is stated that routine issues can be handled by the relevant officials, and policy issues should be referred to the Board of Directors. However, it seems that the determination of what is a routine issue and what is a policy issue is largely left to the relevant officials. A detailed study of the revised Board of Directors Rules and Regulations, with regard to the status of the various committees and the extent of the administrative power that can be exercised by the heads of the various departments, is contained in the appendix to this chapter (Note 10). A comparison of the old rules and regulations, as well as certain proposed reforms that have been considered, are also mentioned in that appendix. (To be continued)

Free Talk

Quotes from Ma Xiangbo, an Old Man of Ninety-Three

The So-Called Diplomatic Skills 85

— Jing Ji

Old Man Xiang is as usual, sitting in his chair reading a book. This is a good habit of not letting the day pass idly! I knocked on the door and went in to report some things. After finishing, Old Man Xiang said, take a look at this "Yan Family Instructions"!

I responded and took it to read. It turned out to be about: During the Northern and Southern Dynasties, parents taught their children to speak Xianbei and play the Huqin, preparing to serve the foreign princes and officials who had taken over China! After reading it, I remained silent.

Old Man Xiang then sighed, "Now Chinese children also learn foreign languages and play mahjong!" I felt a little uneasy listening to this! Old Man Xiang then told me that the customs of Western diplomats were even more unbearable, giving many examples. Here is an interesting story:

"Paris wine, drunk in London, has to be cheap and good. Think about the behind-the-scenes dealings! Many scholars, when they reach a dead end, go to rely on diplomats. The ambassador or minister still has to examine his character, whether he really has some knowledge. As a result, if there is no good position, he is assigned to be a doorman. Think about it, isn't that humiliating? Not at all!

Because all the items shipped to the embassies or legations abroad are routinely tax-exempt, London can drink cheap and good Paris wine! When the embassy can't finish drinking, the doorman and other staff can sell some to the local gentry! The poor scholar acting as a doorman can originally make connections with visiting gentlemen through his conversation, so the problem of livelihood is solved!

This is just using so-called diplomatic skills to do something interesting."

Hoe Life 86

— Xu Rongyu

丨 Put down the gun and pick up the hoe 丨

"Labor can improve health." "Mental labor is not as pleasant as physical labor." These two sentences are indeed correct! I, who am used to holding a pen, have recently put down the pen and picked up a hoe. But I hold this hoe not really to learn to be a gardener, but for two reasons:

First: "It is good to be vigorous when old" is a saying that everyone knows and hopes for. I am approaching middle age, and relying on the pen for a living, I rarely exercise my body or have the opportunity to move my muscles and bones. If you squeeze into a group of young people and practice some sports, others will definitely say you are crazy. Taking this opportunity to hoe the fields, I can exercise my body and strengthen my muscles and bones.

Second: "Go to the countryside" is a saying that everyone shouts. But the extravagance and comfort of city life make you unwilling to leave. Now I have come to the countryside. If I don't hold a hoe, I am not a real country person.

I know that these two reasons are not very thorough. However, I, who hold a pen, although I do not benefit the country, I do not harm society. Now I have put down the pen. If the soldiers who hold guns are willing to put down their guns and pick up hoes, that would be a great joy!

Speaking of holding a hoe, it was a bit painful at first. In the first few days, blisters appeared on my hands; after a few days, my limbs ached. When calluses grew on my hands and my limbs recovered and felt comfortable, holding a hoe and wielding it freely was much easier than holding a pen!

The harvest under the hoe is nothing more than melons, beans, and vegetables. The crystallization of labor is naturally fresher and more precious than those sold in the market. After sweating a lot, large melons, clusters of beans, and sweet and tender vegetables give you a considerable reward, which is also worth it.

The comrades in the countryside who hold hoes are muddle-headed and still have ancient customs, and they are much happier than the comrades who hold pens and guns. They get up in the morning, go to a small teahouse to drink a pot of tea, talk about mountains and seas; in the evening, after finishing work, go to a small tavern to drink a few cups of white wine, and go home to sleep, which is very much in line with the saying "work at sunrise, rest at sunset."

Dear readers! I am not promoting rural life just because I have come to the countryside, and desperately writing beautiful articles about the countryside. In fact, the scenery of the countryside is so interesting, and our country has always been "established on agriculture," so it is worth promoting!

The Sorrow of Chinese Soldiers 87

— Xiaobing

丨 To whom to appeal 丨

No salary for a year, eating only coarse rice, vegetables, and tofu all day long, wearing those two smelly military uniforms. Not going to resist foreign enemies and defend the country, but acting as private tools, killing each other.

Because they have no money to use, some who are ignorant of the consequences steal and sell guns and ammunition. Once discovered, they are arrested, tied to the execution ground, and shot to maintain military discipline and warn others.

Excerpts from the Panchen Lama's Teachings (Part 1) 88

— Recorded by Di Pingzi

Bearing the inner Dharma, all the great lay Buddhists who initiated the Kalachakra Vajra Dharma assembly are aware of the previous letter, which has now been delivered. Now, I will briefly contribute my humble opinion. Because of the continuous wars and disasters in various places, all sentient beings are suffering immeasurable pain. Tracing the cause, it is due to ignorance of the truth of good and evil. Now, if we want to thoroughly investigate its principles so that everyone knows the importance of taking and abandoning, this is the business of those who study inner learning. I respectfully submit that my teacher, Shakyamuni Tathagata, is also an incarnation. From his time as an ordinary person, he has regarded all sentient beings as far superior to himself, cherishing and protecting them. For the sake of others, he did not hesitate to give up his most precious life. Moreover, he was meticulous in his actions, never doing anything evil, no matter how small. If anyone harmed him, even if it was unbearable, he would persevere in forbearance, cultivate all good deeds, be diligent without end, eliminate distractions, keep his mind constantly in concentration, reach the fundamental truth of the Dharma, and wisdom would appear.

Practice, such as the six perfections practiced in turn, to the end, cutting off all afflictions and the two obscurations of knowledge, manifesting the power of the four bodies, clearly knowing all knowable objects without a hair's breadth of concealment, purifying all diseases, possessing all merits, still without even a trace of suffering, even the name of suffering has been extinguished. Therefore, he constantly dwells in the bliss of the Dharma. However, he is not satisfied with the vows of his past intentions, vowing to lead all sentient beings into his own samadhi of bliss, speaking of all kinds of suffering. With such a mind, he constantly and diligently benefits sentient beings, responding to all the opportunities and inclinations of sentient beings, and speaking of the common and uncommon Dharma. Moreover, all the Dharma he speaks is not based on what others say, but according to his own enlightened realm, speaking truthfully. Therefore, all of us sentient beings should follow the Buddha's teachings and practice as instructed.

The most important thing in learning Buddhism is to have great faith in the teacher, Buddha. If you want to have faith in the Buddha, you should first study the deeds of the Buddha's incarnations. If you gain something from studying them, faith will naturally arise. Then, the idea of treasuring and protecting the rare and precious Dharma will also arise. Once this mind is established, you will naturally be able to cultivate all good deeds diligently and tirelessly, and it will also increase constantly. Let's get rid of the bad habits.

The essence of the Dharma lies in the mind. Reaching the essence of the Dharma lies in recognizing your own mind and saving your own nature. I and all sentient beings, because we know self-sacrifice, generate greed for all fame and fortune, praise, and relatives and friends. On the contrary, if others harm my virtue, wealth, or treasures, or prevent them from increasing, I will not tolerate it and will generate regret. Therefore, I do not tend towards all good deeds, and I do not know all evil deeds. This is because I am deluded by ignorance, the three poisons increase daily, and the delusions of pride, jealousy, and wrong views also grow with them. This is the total cause of the accumulation of all sufferings.

If you know your own mind and save yourself, all afflictions will naturally cease. Once afflictions cease, bliss will naturally arise. This is the natural principle.

A Friend Comes from the Pseudo-State · Zhu · Zuo · Fen

A friend came from the pseudo-state, telling a tragic and moving story.

The facts are like this:

In Changchun, there are many alleys with many gambling houses and opium dens openly opened, exclusively for the entertainment of Korean and Chinese hooligans.

On the day the Nine-One-Five pseudo-state treaty was signed, a Chinese and a Korean twisted to the Japanese special military gendarmerie because of gambling debts. "What country are you from?" "Manchukuo!" "What's the matter?" "He is a slave of a defeated country (referring to the Korean), and I am also a slave of a defeated country (!). Why doesn't he pay me back the money he owes me!"

The Japanese police officer laughed loudly, took out two yuan from his side, "Take it!" The Chinese gambler respectfully accepted it and said repeatedly, "Yes! Yes!" The Japanese police officer said, "He will slowly pay you back what he owes you!" Then he said to the Korean, "You should also slowly pay him back. You slaves of defeated countries are equal."

Both slaves of the defeated country came out very happily!

Postal Companions Entering the Pass (21) 90

— Seeking Happiness

When Tong Yizhen spoke of the most sad place, he couldn't help but want to cry loudly. Lu Boqin stood like a stone statue, unexpectedly giving a decisive answer: "This, don't be sad, I can answer you immediately. I have made up my mind, let's go into the pass together." At this

time, Tong Yizhen was looking up at Lu Boqin's face with tearful eyes. Suddenly hearing this happy sentence, he was so happy that he laughed and held his arm to ask in detail:

"Really? I didn't expect you to be decisive today! But I still want to ask you, the decision for your postal staff to enter the pass was already made several days ago. The previous two times we talked about this, you were still unwilling to loosen your mouth. Why did you think of doing this at this moment?" "Yizhen! Haven't you heard me say before that everything should be based on your happiness as the premise? If you rashly follow me, it will be of no benefit to you, and it will be too damaging to your reputation. I thought that the previous difficulties still had hope of being saved, so there was no need to rush to take this last resort. Even this time I have to leave you to return to the mainland, although I am very reluctant; but in the end I still thought that if you stayed here alone, it shouldn't be absolutely dangerous, and maybe I can still leave quietly in the end; but today's matter is greatly different! These people who want to harm you are like wild beasts that cannot be reasoned with, and what is in front of you is the most serious moment between humans and beasts. How can I hesitate for another moment, watching you fall into the group of wild beasts? Therefore, I have no choice but to make this decision from the perspective of power, without regard to all common interests." Lu Boqin explained his theory very resolutely. "But how should we go?" Tong Yizhen still had to ask clearly. "Fortunately, things are also very coincidental; today I also received news from the bureau that the Postmaster has received an order from the government to close the post office and lead all the staff into the pass. Japan has also agreed to sign passports, and we can take their Fengshan Railway train. As long as we have the date of boarding, we can secretly board the train together." Lu Boqin also had a more practical way. Finally, Tong Yizhen remembered all the obstacles to his departure and proposed to discuss how to deal with them with Lu Boqin in detail? A secret plan was also set.
