Commercial News

On Nominalist Philosophy 91

— Tianfang

Speaking of philosophy, it evokes a long string of terms from various schools: "Monism," "Dualism," "Pluralism," "Materialism," "Idealism," "Sentimentalism," etc., but oddly enough, the term "Nominalist Philosophy" is never heard. This is the fault of past historians. In reality, this doctrine has been passed down for a very long time and is highly revered. People who uphold this doctrine are truly everywhere. Now, I will briefly outline its main points for future compilers of philosophical histories to refer to.

Speaking of the origins of this doctrine, because it has been passed down for so long, written records have been lost. Some say it originated in A. Others say it originated with Xun Kuang, Gongsun Long, and their followers. Some say it was established by Confucius, because he wrote the "Spring and Autumn Annals," which terrified rebellious ministers and villainous sons, and he also said, "What is necessary is to rectify names." This seems relatively close. However, Mencius said that the account in the Book of Documents of King Wu's conquest of Zhou, where blood flowed so much that pestles floated, is unreliable. So, great... It seems that during the Three Dynasties, there was something like a news policy, like today's information warfare, which can serve as evidence for the existence of this doctrine. In short, it can be asserted that it existed in ancient times and is even more prevalent today. As for the traces of its transmission, they are quite vague, and I will leave it to gentlemen with a penchant for textual research and history to investigate. Here, I can only omit it.

Secondly, speaking of the benefits of this doctrine, the first is that it can deal with others, and the second is that it can comfort oneself. For example, if Wang Xiao'er is angered by Li A'si, he holds a grudge in his heart. He then draws a turtle on the wall and writes next to it, "Li A'si is a little turtle." He looks at it himself, and Li A'si has really turned into a little turtle. Thus, his anger subsides, his hatred disappears, and this small dispute comes to an end. If Wang Xiao'er were to be replaced by someone who could write, he would pick up a pen and write an article insinuating and slandering, and publish it externally, or write an anonymous letter to threaten him. As long as the other party is slightly affected, his wishes will be fulfilled. There is no need for it to actually happen, nor is it necessary to realize what you said with real swords and guns – that would be too much trouble. If you want to save the country, then you might as well first set a program, and then issue a declaration, saying how the country should be saved. Outsiders will admire it, and you yourself won't think it's anything special when you read it. At this time, if you feel that your anger has not subsided, then you can shout a slogan at will, such as "Down with ××," "Kill all ××," "Long-term resistance," "Swear to resist Japan," and the like. The more fierce the words, the more tragic the tone, the better. You don't have to shout it on the street; it's also okay in a mansion or villa. Speaking of the function of relieving anger, shouting slogans and singing actually have the same effect. Therefore, speaking of the application of this doctrine, it is truly boundless. For example, if you have a child at home who cries at night and cannot sleep, then you can write a line on red paper, "The Heavenly Emperor is bright, the Earthly Emperor is bright..." and paste it on the street. Or, if you have a severe cold, you can also write a line in the same way, "Selling a severe cold, success at first sight," and paste it in the toilet or on a telephone pole. Although your child may not necessarily fall asleep, and your cold may not necessarily get better, at least you yourself are comforted. If you are a merchant, then please do not be stingy with those extremely self-sacrificing words, such as "Regardless of cost," "Selling at cost," and the like. You also don't have to worry that you don't sound like a merchant; no one will question you. You should also be good at using terms such as "Bargain," "Discount," and so on. From the grand opening bargain to the clearance sale, in the newspapers and verbally, just keep saying "Great Bargain, Special Bargain." Once, twice, ten weeks, five weeks, it will definitely not conflict with your original profit-making purpose. This is the function of names. Or, if someone criticizes you for going to the movies every day, you can say, "Entertaining doesn't mean forgetting the national crisis." If you don't have a son and want to take a concubine, you can say, "Of the three unfilial acts, having no descendants is the greatest." Alas, the use of names is great indeed.

Science

Talking About Electrons (One of a Series of Radio Talks) 93

— Enthusiastic

We know that a bowl of water can be divided into two bowls. We naturally believe that a drop of water, when divided to the point where it cannot be divided further, can no longer be divided in the name of water. But we can still use scientific methods to divide this drop of water into two kinds of atoms. Can atoms not be divided further? No. Every atom has a nucleus and many electrons. Of course, it is possible to divide the atom further into a nucleus and individual electrons. Now, if we take everything in this world and analyze it step by step, the final result is that everything comes down to the nucleus of the atom and electrons. They are currently considered the original substances that make up this world.

If we use electricity to explain, then in every atom, its nucleus always carries a positive charge; the electron always carries a negative charge. These electrons, which create everything in the world

The shape and characteristics of the substances are the same. That is to say, the electrons in a gold atom and the electrons in a silver atom are not different. However, the number of electrons contained in two different atoms is very different. The reason why the same electrons constitute different atoms lies in this.

So, why are the numbers of electrons different in different atoms? This is because the amount of positive charge carried by the nucleus of the atom is different. For example, if the nucleus of atom A carries more positive charge than the nucleus of atom B, it needs more electrons because it needs to equalize the amount of positive charge it carries, so it naturally needs more than atom B. If an atom loses some of its inherent electrons due to external pressure, then the positive charge emitted by the nucleus inside it becomes excessive. This excess of positive charge

Then, he tried his best to attract electrons from other places to maintain his original equilibrium. In our spare time, we occasionally play a trick: we take a piece of silk to wipe a piece of glass, and when the glass gets hot, we use it to attract paper scraps. This is the reason. The glass loses some of its electrons as a result of friction. There are electrons inside the paper scraps. It's just that the paper scraps can't let go and let the electrons be sucked away by the glass. So, it's like you pulling and me tugging, and the result is that the lighter one suffers. The paper scraps are sucked away by the glass.

If You Want to Do a Good Job, You Must First Sharpen Your Tools 94

— Yong Sen Works

Page 17

Based on what was said above, let's imagine that we are now using a scientific method to confine many nuclei of electrons carrying positive charges on one side. They all need a large number of electrons to combine with them, and confine many electrons carrying negative charges on the other side. They are all waiting for something to lead them so that they have a place to return. When we put these two sides together, every electron rushes to the nucleus, and every nucleus absorbs electrons with all its might. A violent change is inevitable. This violent change will not stop until all the electrons on the electron side are gone. The batteries we usually use have this function when they are energized. However, the explanation of electricity was already available before the invention of electrons. Scientists used water as an analogy, believing that current flows from the anode to the cathode, just like water flows from high ground to low ground. Of course, this explanation has no other basis than association. However, scientists have been using this explanation for a long time, and many theorems are based on this explanation, so there is no way to abolish it. Therefore, there is a very ridiculous contradictory fact in electrical science now: the current flows from the anode to the cathode, and the electrons flow from the cathode to the anode. But although this fact is ridiculous, we must always keep it in mind when we study it.

Society Improvement Discussion Group

Questions on New Families and Social Improvement 95

—

Question by Gao Zhuoyun

After reading Mr. Wang Mingxing's article "My Opinion on the Standards of New Families" in the Shanghai Shen Bao supplement, I have some doubts and would like to express my humble opinion for readers to discuss. Mr. Wang said, "The evils of Chinese society are said to be myriad: the important reason, in my humble opinion, lies not in the family but in the government's inability to enable people to live and work in peace and solve the problem of people's livelihood." It is certainly true that the evils of Chinese society lie in the government's inability to enable people to live and work in peace! But it is not true that it does not lie in the family. After all, the organization of society and the people are of primary importance. The depth of the people's knowledge, the strength of their physical fitness, and the goodness or badness of their habits are all self-evident in their importance to the country. If we want to advance the people's knowledge, strengthen their physical fitness, and improve their habits, then we must improve education, promote physical education, and reform entertainment! Which one can be lacking? Therefore, if we want to cultivate good citizens, we must have a good environment. After a child is born, the family is its first environment. Whether the family is good or bad has a great impact on the child's future! Children are the pillars of future society, and whether children are good or bad is also the same as whether society is good or bad. Mr. Wang said that the unimprovement of society does not lie in the family, what is the truth? People who are raised in a bad environment cannot only not cooperate to improve society, but also hinder those who seek improvement. The difficult birth of our country's revolution is not because of the obstruction of generally outdated thinkers. Sun Yat-sen called for psychological construction at the beginning of the revolution for a reason. Rousseau said, "A child who is wrongly taught is further away from wisdom than a child who has not been educated." It can be seen that it is especially important to be cautious in educating children in the first step, and the family is the place where children receive preliminary education, so it cannot be said that the proposal to renovate the family is not an essential suggestion. Although the current political situation is not on the right track, it is truly what we feel pain and heartache about. However, to abandon all progress because the political situation is not on the right track is no different from giving up eating because of choking! As the saying goes, "Keep the big picture in mind and start with the small things." Sun Yat-sen also said, "We must aspire to do great things, not to be great officials." He earnestly warned us to fulfill our responsibilities as citizens and work hard. Since we are powerless and powerless common people, we have no right to interfere with the major plans of the government, so we should also seek improvement in what we can and are able to do. After all, everyone has a family, and everyone can improve the family. Therefore, I intend that the political clarity of the country should begin with the improvement of the family, just as autonomy begins with the local area. In short, it is faster for the government to seek the big and difficult things and for the people to seek the small and easy things, with everyone working together, than to entrust the entire responsibility to the government to seek social progress.

Casual Talks

Scattered Notes by the Pillow 96

— Wen Bing

Generally speaking, in student days, everyone hopes that teachers will take leave and reduce classes. After leaving school and entering the door of society, everyone regrets that they should not have, but it is too late to regret.

It seems that the Russian blind poet Eroshanko said, "The Chinese have rickshaws pulled by people (Note: This was invented by the Japanese, so it is also called a 'Eastern car'), which is really a rare thing!" I think if his eyes were not blind, he would see the scene of the rickshaw pullers sweating in the hot summer, washing their faces, and the passengers sitting comfortably, and I wonder what he would think?

I often hear people saying that two out of every three sentences end with "so-so". On the surface, it is purely a habit that comes out of the mouth involuntarily, and it cannot be said to be anything conscious. But upon careful consideration, this is simply a manifestation of a Chinese inferiority. Everything is "so-so", which has led to the symbol of slow progress and badness in personnel and society. When I first learned English, the teacher seemed to say, "The purpose of reading foreign texts is to understand foreign countries and learn their strengths." But now, college students use it as the most fashionable social skill. When Chinese people meet Chinese people, they also speak foreign languages ​​in a boastful manner, as if they cannot show that they are upper-class people without it. It's really inexplicable!

I usually knew that Chinese planes were only suitable for delivering mail and transporting important people. During the Shanghai war, they didn't even dare to do this and stopped for several days. Thinking of this, I couldn't help but shudder.

The only hope of merchants is that business is good. To put it bluntly, they want to make more money. Therefore, clothing store owners are afraid that people's old clothes will not be removed, and hotel owners are afraid that drinkers will not get drunk. By analogy, drugstore owners are afraid that people will not get sick, and coffin shop owners are afraid that not enough people will die. This is probably the reason why merchants are at the tail end of the four classes of people.

After going to Nanjing, I realized that this so-called historical city, the revolutionary capital, was originally nothing more than that. The unemployed people blocked the roads, and the most developed businesses were hotels, bathhouses, and barbershops. The muddy streets were so narrow that two people would bump shoulders when walking side by side. In disappointment, I was reminded of the collapsing entire Chinese society. The decline of one city is only a small thing.

No matter what students do at school, it is always difficult to mobilize the whole group to participate quickly. Only when it comes to meals can I guarantee that no one will be absent unless there are special circumstances. If there are outstanding female students dancing at the variety show, which is a feast for the eyes, then they will be even more quick to arrive. It turns out that Confucius said, "Food and sex are human nature." People who have a position in society often deliberately dress old, while people who are new to society love to dress gorgeously. All of this is caused by the gaze of social people and an improper pathology.

Many friends say that they wish to be reborn as women in the next life because women in today's society are particularly cheap. In any aspect, they can be irresponsible as long as they have one condition: being beautiful and coquettish. From this, we can know the so-called status of women in today's society.

Living in a Drunken Dream

Flower Club Poison 97

— Ru Li

"Playing the flower club, nine copper coins pay one yuan, when luck is good, one dollar can get more than thirty yuan, what a great thing this is!" A few men in short shirts were talking with relish at the tea table of the tiger stove. At this time, a small worker, A'si, sat next to him and listened in a daze, thinking that this matter could make it so that I, as a small worker, am busy all day long but only earn a few cents, how can there be a day to get rich? Immediately stood up and ran to a broken and low thatched house in an alley to play the flower club. When he returned home, he was so happy that he kept laughing and said to his wife, "We are going to get rich soon, we can get more than thirty yuan today!"

When the flower club opened in the evening, A'si hurried to check the numbers. He knew that he had not won. A'si was stunned. The person who opened the flower club said to him, "It's nothing strange if you don't win once. If you play a few times in a row, you will win." A'si listened and his heart blossomed with joy and a smile on his face. He took out a dollar from the pocket of his tattered and dirty clothes and bet on one number. From then on, he gave up his original career as a small worker. Every day when he ate and slept, he silently recited in his head whether it was better to bet on "Pearl" or "Must Get". Sometimes he sighed in his dreams, "I got it, I got rich!" A'si played a total of dozens of times, and every time he lost. A few days ago, he suddenly went crazy and shouted loudly, "I can't always win like this, how good is the flower club? I've run out of money at home, and my clothes have been pawned. I heard that it is very accurate to have people's heads to entrust dreams." But where can he get people's heads? So he went even more crazy. He didn't know everything. He ran to the kitchen, took a kitchen knife, and was really going to kill someone. Now he has been caught by the police and taken to the police station. His wife has become a beggar.

Alas, everyone, the above is indeed a true story, not something I made up. Now I want to solemnly say a few words to my dear compatriots: you must know that there are more than thirty numbers in the flower club, and only one number is opened. There are also behind-the-scenes manipulations in it. Where can you get it? Taking the money of blood and sweat to play the flower club is like committing suicide with a sword. All those who are poisoned by the flower club will eventually be separated from their wives and children, and even commit suicide. Is it pitiful or not? Wake up, don't dream of gold, do my proper business, and live my happy life.

The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant Ma Laoba for two-eighths, and Fu Yunfei and Fu Xingwang shall each bear three-eighths. ▲ Wang Jingyuan and Feng Deming, et al. are involved in a lawsuit for requesting payment of rent (Main Text): The defendant Feng Deming shall pay the plaintiff rent of 80 yuan in silver dollars. The plaintiff's claim against the defendant Shen Dingji is rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant Feng Deming. ▲ Lu Pan, et al. and Zhang Runsen, et al. are involved in a lawsuit for requesting payment of ground rent and relocation (Main Text): The defendant Zhang Runsen shall pay the plaintiff ground rent of 280 yuan in silver dollars. If unable to repay, the defendant Wang Jinbo shall be responsible for the substitute payment. The remaining claims of the plaintiff are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff for one-tenth and the defendant Zhang Runsen for nine-tenths. ▲ Meng Shutao and Chen Wang's are involved in a lawsuit for requesting payment of rent arrears and relocation (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff rent arrears of 22 yuan and 40 cents. The remaining claims of the plaintiff are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne equally by both parties. Deming and Qi Zhu are involved in a case for requesting payment of a hui loan (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff a hui loan of 40 yuan in silver dollars. The remaining claims of the plaintiff are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff for one-third and the defendant for two-thirds. ▲ Leng Xinfu and Qian Zijie are involved in a lawsuit for requesting payment of rent arrears and relocation (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff rent arrears of 256 yuan in silver dollars and 32 cents in small silver dollars, and relocate from the house. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff. The judgment in the first item listed above shall be declared provisionally enforceable. ▲ Tan Jinpu and Chen Zhongxin are involved in a lawsuit for requesting payment of a bill (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff, the manager, the amount of 1,050 yuan in silver dollars from the Xininghai Slaughtering Company, plus interest at an annual rate of 6% from the date of issuance of the respective bills until the date of execution. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Zhang Zhichun and Li Hongxun, et al. are involved in a lawsuit for requesting payment of rent arrears (Main Text): The defendant Li Hongxun shall pay the plaintiff rent arrears of 552 taels of silver. The defendant Guo Baozhi shall pay the plaintiff rent arrears of 248 taels of silver. The defendant Fang Bing shall pay the plaintiff rent arrears of 800 taels of silver. The defendant Jian Kechuan shall pay the plaintiff rent arrears of 840 taels of silver. The defendant Yuan Yongsheng shall pay the plaintiff rent arrears of 500 taels of silver. The defendant Wang Heyuan shall pay the plaintiff rent arrears of 50 taels of silver. The defendant An Shoucu shall pay the plaintiff rent arrears of 50 taels of silver. The defendant Fan Mengju shall pay the plaintiff rent arrears of 100 taels of silver. The defendant Juan Wenfu shall pay the plaintiff rent arrears of 130 taels of silver. The defendant He Changzhen shall pay the plaintiff rent arrears of 195 taels of silver. The defendant Lin Xianqi shall pay the plaintiff rent arrears of 260 taels of silver. The defendant Gu Wensheng shall pay the plaintiff rent arrears of 110 taels of silver. The litigation costs shall be borne equally by the defendants Li Mingxun, Fang Bing, and Jian Kechuan for three-tenths, and by the defendants Wang Heyuan, Liang Shoucu, and Fan Mengju for one-tenth. ▲ Song Xingsheng for Li Jiting in the case for requesting repayment of public funds (Main Text): The appeal is dismissed. The second instance litigation fee is borne by the appellant. ▲ Zhao Amao, et al. and Zhu Guisheng are involved in a lawsuit for requesting redemption of land (Main Text): The plaintiff's claim is rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne equally by the plaintiffs. ▲ Hongxingcheng Rice Store and Zhou Laoying are involved in a lawsuit for requesting payment of public funds (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff 1,929 yuan, 5 jiao, and 2 fen in silver. This amount shall be repaid at a rate of 100 yuan per month until fully repaid. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Zhu Zhengfa and Chen Asi are involved in a lawsuit for requesting repayment of debt (Main Text): The appeal is dismissed. The second instance litigation costs are borne by the appellant. ▲ Cao Yungeng and Zhou Yunlong are involved in a lawsuit for requesting repayment of rent arrears and relocation (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff rent arrears of 666 yuan and terminate the lease contract and relocate immediately. The remaining claims of the plaintiff are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff for four-tenths and the defendant for six-tenths. ▲ Shen Ziming and Wang Jiting are involved in a case for requesting payment of rent and relocation (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff rent of 65 yuan in silver dollars and shall relocate from the house. The litigation costs, except for the four-fifths of the settlement portion that shall be resolved separately, one-fifth shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Jiang Zhonglian and Ma Zhending are involved in a rent arrears case. Defendant Ma Zhending shall pay the plaintiff rent of 56 yuan in silver dollars. Xu Baohui shall pay the plaintiff rent of 78 yuan in silver dollars and also 76 cents in small silver dollars. Dai Taozi shall pay the plaintiff rent of 114 yuan in silver dollars and also 114 cents in small silver dollars, and all shall relocate from the house. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendants in proportion. ▲ Yuhe Rice Store and Hong Zhaochu are involved in a lawsuit for requesting repayment of rice money (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff the rice price of 2,200 yuan in silver dollars, plus interest at an annual rate of 5% from February 1st of this year until the date of execution. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. (Above from October 22nd)

Civil Judgment Public Notice: Zhu Ruichen and Zhang Baofu are involved in a case for requesting repayment of guarantee money (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff the cargo money of 83 yuan and 92 cents in silver dollars. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. To: Defendant Zhang Baofu. ▲ Dong Gao's and Shao Wenrong are involved in a loan case. This court has scheduled a public hearing for 9 AM on November 14th. The defendant is ordered to appear in court on time for the debate and not delay. This public notice is hereby issued. To: Defendant Shao Wenrong. ▲ Judgment: Pan Changpei, et al. and Li Hongenlian are involved in a lawsuit for hui money and repayment of money (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff Pan Changpei a hui loan of 300 yuan in silver dollars, Yu Fuchang a hui loan of 88 yuan in silver dollars, and Zhao Zelin a loan of 105 yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. To: Defendant Li Hongenlian. ▲ Haiji Company and Xieji Jipengxing Pledge Money Case (Main Text): The defendant Xieji Jiyaxing (Chicken and Duck Shop), Rao Hanzhang, shall repay the plaintiff the pledge money of 3,000 taels of silver, plus interest at the agreed rate of 1.25% per month from January 1st, 1932 until the date of

execution. If unable to repay, the defendant Shao Yunxuan shall be responsible for the substitute payment. The remaining claims of the plaintiff are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant Xieji Jiyaxing. ▲ Mao Rongchu and Wang Xuetang are involved in a lawsuit for requesting compensation for damages (Main Text): The plaintiff's claim and the counterclaim are both rejected. The litigation costs for the main lawsuit shall be borne by the plaintiff, and the litigation costs for the counterclaim shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Bai Xianzheng and Lu Qisheng are involved in a lawsuit for requesting repayment of a loan (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff the loan of 1,800 yuan in silver dollars, plus interest at the agreed rate of 1.6% per month from December 16th, 1931 until the date of execution. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Shen Danzhen and Xuan Changui are involved in a lawsuit for requesting repayment of renovation expenses (Main Text): The defendant Xuan Changui shall repay the plaintiff rent arrears of 168 yuan in silver dollars and relocate from the house. If unable to pay the rent arrears, the defendant Huachengxing Yongji Tea and Food Shop shall be responsible for the substitute payment. The remaining claims of the plaintiff are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. (Above from October 24th)
